Current Affairs Commentary

Forty-Two to One

(1) The Prestige of the League of Nations

Japan is barbaric. The puppet state is utterly ugly. Anyone who understands the details of the Sino-Japanese conflict cannot help but marvel at it as a historical farce. Uchiya Kōsai, the protagonist who instigated the September 18th Incident, has taken office as Minister of Foreign Affairs, transforming from a peaceful rubber [toy] to a steel puppet used by the military. His toughness and unreasonableness truly befit him as a loyal representative of Japanese militarism. He despises justice and tramples on the three northeastern provinces, believing that the world should be dominated by Japan alone. He is determined to kill all Chinese people to safeguard his so-called lifeline. Although our country has consistently made concessions, countries around the world have become greatly dissatisfied. The international situation has undergone a major transformation.

After the Nineteen-Nation Committee drafted its report, the Japanese imperialist plot to advance into Rehe, peer into Luandong, and disrupt North China became even more apparent. Our country has suffered deeply and can no longer tolerate it. Rising up to fight is inevitable. Striving to resist is the most justifiable action. The countries of Britain and France, for the sake of the League of Nations' prestige and the international balance, can no longer delay and allow Japan's iron heel to crush East Asia. Therefore, on the 24th of this month, the League of Nations General Assembly, after careful consideration of the rights and interests, fearing not Japan's threat to withdraw from the League of Nations, passed the report drafted by the Nineteen-Nation Committee by a vote of forty-two to one. No country openly supported Japan's claims, and no country recognized Japan's so-called "Royal Way." This General Assembly at least made countries around the world clearly recognize Japan's true face. At the same time, it declared that the Manchurian puppet state was indeed fabricated by the Japanese warlords and can no longer deceive the world with a peaceful facade. China is openly at war with Japan to resist the trampling of violence, and its momentum will be boosted by the moral support of the world.

(2) The Application of Article 16 of the Covenant

The reason why Japan discards everything and acts so recklessly is partly because it deceives itself into thinking that China is weak and unable to resist, and partly because it takes advantage of the conflict between Britain and the United States, and the discord between Britain and the Soviet Union, believing that no power will be able to restrain Japan. Thirdly, it deceives itself into thinking that the League of Nations is only a moral organization that relies solely on words and has no ability. Therefore, the resolution of thirteen votes to one on October 34th of the previous year was opposed solely by Japan, and not only was the resolution not established, but the H soldiers continued to occupy Liaoning and Jilin, and the situation expanded to Jilin, Heilongjiang, Jinzhou, and Yi County. Recently, it also occupied Shanhaiguan and flew to the Rehe border.

Although the League of Nations calls on the world for peace, the economic panic has yet to find a way out. Countries, for their own sake and for the sake of international balance, cannot use force. Japan's violation of the treaty and breach of faith are obvious. Now it has withdrawn from the League of Nations and is launching a large-scale attack on Rehe. The League of Nations has no weapons in its hands and is unable to stop the Japanese army's advance. How can it expect its proposals to be implemented? Even if the United States of North America and the Soviet Union both willingly participate in negotiations, it is feared that they may still not be able to restrain Japan's recklessness. But there is a way. Article 16 of the League of Nations Covenant clearly stipulates:

[Should any Member of the League resort to war in disregard of its covenants under Articles 12, 13 or 15]

then it shall ipso facto be deemed to have committed an act of war against all other Members of the League, which hereby undertake immediately to subject it to the severance of all [trade] or [financial] relations, the prohibition of all intercourse between their nationals and the nationals of the covenant-breaking State, etc. ]

[In such case the Council shall recommend to the several Governments concerned what effective military, naval or air force the Members of the League shall severally contribute to the armed forces to be used to protect the covenants of the League.]

Whether this measure can be implemented is something that does not require a wise man to know. But the right and ability to implement it are not in the distant headquarters of the League of Nations in Western Europe, but in the Republic of China, which is suffering the most.

(3) Can Justice Triumph Over Power?

Since the September 18th Incident, our country has been seeking [justice]. Now that justice has been obtained, the means to enforce this [justice] cannot be expected from the League of Nations. After Japan withdraws from the League of Nations, it will not be bound by the covenant, and it will no longer care about the League of Nations' decisions. It will rely solely on its army and navy to act recklessly everywhere. Just look at how that country's army is conscripting first-year soldiers onto the battlefield, and its navy is borrowing from large-scale exercises to demonstrate its power. Its desire to explode the Manchurian powder keg is obvious. Its consciousness of provoking war is also very clear. Some people compare us to Belgium at the beginning of the European war. But that is not true. Because our country has the support of [justice] and bears the responsibility of implementing this justice. In terms of our own interests, we should exert all our strength, use iron fists to drive out thieves, and use red blood to defend [justice].

At the beginning of the Northeast Incident, the Japanese imperialists used the excuse of preventing the Red Russians from moving south to win over England and incite France. They reaped the benefits and swept through the three provinces, preparing for war in every step. As for suppressing the national revolutionary movement, it was also one of the smoke bombs. After more than a year, the countries have realized Japan's cunning and realized that it is using this

League of Nations Advisory Committee Discusses Banning Arms Exports to the Far East

The British Government is Responsible for Contacting Relevant Countries

The United States and Russia are Actively Considering Participating in the Issue

(Geneva) The Advisory Committee, created by yesterday's League of Nations Assembly to monitor the China Dispute and assist the League of Nations Assembly in fulfilling its functions, held its opening ceremony at 11:00 AM this morning, which lasted for 35 minutes. It decided to instruct the Secretariat to send letters to the United States and Russia inviting them to participate in its work. After the recess, the Secretariat immediately issued the invitations in accordance with the instructions. The Advisory Committee also discussed the arms export ban. British representative Eden asked the members to consider this issue individually. Eden suggested that it would be best to form a subcommittee of countries with special relations to study it. Countries expressed sympathy for this proposal, promising to study the matter immediately so that it could be discussed together at the next meeting.

The United States and Russia Participate in the Situation

It is Widely Believed that the United States Will Accept the Invitation

The reply accepting the invitation to participate in the work of the Advisory Committee may be issued soon, and will not be delayed because the new president has not yet taken office. US representative Gilbert has been frequently appearing in the gallery of the League of Nations, and may be the US representative to the Advisory Committee. The reply from Russian Foreign Affairs Official Litvinov may be slightly delayed. Litvinov is currently in Geneva, but is scheduled to return to Moscow tomorrow in order to meet with key Soviet Russian figures to make a concrete decision on assisting the work of the League of Nations and joining the Advisory Committee, which will expand the twenty-one member committee into a twenty-three member committee.

Britain is Contacting to Ban Arms Exports

After the Advisory Committee adjourned, it issued a public statement, which stated, "The Advisory Committee established by yesterday's League of Nations Assembly met this morning, chaired by Hymans. It was decided to invite the United States and Russia to participate in its work in accordance with the resolution of the League of Nations Assembly. The Committee has learned that the British government has contacted other relevant governments regarding the export of arms to the Far East. The Committee asks the British government to inform it of the developments in this matter from time to time, as this matter is closely related to the work of the Committee. Chairman Hymans stated that he was chairing this meeting of the Advisory Committee in his capacity as chairman of the League of Nations Assembly. The Committee decided to temporarily postpone the chairman issue to the next meeting because Hymans expressed an opinion." (25th Reuters Dispatch)

Resolutions of the Assembly

(Geneva) At 5 p.m. today, the League of Nations Assembly resumed its session. Chinese representative Gu Weijun spoke, requesting the League of Nations to help China overcome its current difficulties, stating that the League should immediately initiate sanctions as stipulated in the Covenant, and detailing the perilous situation in Rehe. He inquired how the League of Nations intended to deal with the imminent crisis in Rehe and then requested the League to authorize a special committee to enable unified action by member and non-member states to prevent the expansion of the war in the Far East, claiming that war was beginning in the Far East and that if countries could not unite and jointly uphold international security, there was a risk of being drawn into disaster. Mr. Gu attempted to refute the speech given by Japanese representative Matsuoka at the morning session, but he was dissuaded by Chairman Hymans, who requested that his remarks be limited to the resolution proposed by the Chairman to organize an advisory committee. Mr. Gu agreed but reserved the right to submit a written refutation of Matsuoka's statement later. Subsequently, the League of Nations Assembly passed the resolution and adjourned at 6:21 p.m. The Japanese representative did not attend, with only two Japanese secretaries from the League of Nations present as observers. The key points of the resolution were: (1) Based on Article 3, Paragraph 3 of the Covenant, the League of Nations cannot ignore the development of the Sino-Japanese conflict. (2) The Secretary-General is instructed to distribute the report to member and non-member states, informing them that the League of Nations Assembly hopes they will take a unified stance. (3) To establish an advisory committee to monitor the situation and assist the League of Nations Assembly in fulfilling its responsibilities under Article 3, Paragraph 3 of the Covenant, and to assist in the development of the conspiracy to monopolize the Chinese market. This is far more sinister than its so-called defense against "redification" and resistance to the Soviet Union. Moreover, since the establishment of the Franco-Soviet Non-Aggression Pact, the situation in Europe has greatly changed. The situation in East Asia is extremely urgent. This is why the League of Nations unanimously passed a resolution denying the legitimacy of "Manchukuo" and confirming that Japan's military actions exceeded the scope of self-defense.

However, Japan remains stubborn and acts recklessly, and cannot be persuaded by reason. Only by using force and providing a bloody lesson can we maintain human peace and ensure the safety of our national lives. And today, the only country in the world that can uphold the League of Nations Covenant and wield the iron fist to teach Japan a lesson is China. Who else?

Countries should adopt a unified attitude. (4) The Advisory Committee will include the members of the Committee of Nineteen, with the addition of the Netherlands and Canada, and will invite the United States and Russia to participate in the work. (5) The League of Nations Assembly will remain in session and may be convened by the President when necessary. (National News Agency telegram, 24th)

Representative Gu Requests the League to Implement Sanctions

Japan's Note Is Simply a Declaration of War

(Geneva) When the League of Nations Assembly continued its session tonight, Chairman Hymans presented a resolution and invited Chinese representative Gu Weijun to speak, but asked him not to touch on the remarks made by Japanese representative Matsuoka this morning. Therefore, Mr. Gu's remarks were limited to the situation in Rehe, describing the dangerous situation in Rehe, and requesting the Assembly to authorize the committee to take necessary steps before adjourning, so that the effective action of member and non-member states could be realized as soon as possible. Dr. Gu stated that the Chinese delegation was prepared to assist the committee's work in any possible way. The recent note from the Japanese delegation to the League of Nations has proven that Japan has absolutely no reason to carry out its ambitions in Rehe. Tang Yulin never declared Rehe independent, but Japan has raised questions about China's sovereignty over its own territory, which directly denies the right of a nation to exist and destroys the basic principles of international law. The Japanese announcement contains warnings; in fact, what right does Japan have to demand that China withdraw its troops defending its territory? "Manchukuo" is not only a puppet state, but also a mask for Japan's militarism. Judging from the conclusions of the Lytton Commission and the League of Nations Assembly report, the so-called Japan-Manchukuo Protocol is actually Japan's confession of guilt. We should focus all our efforts on resisting aggression. The Japanese spokesperson claimed that it was not necessary, and Japan's statement that it did not want to attack Beiping and Tianjin was Japan's way of foreshadowing its desire to obtain a second object. Yesterday's Japanese note was simply a declaration of war. The Assembly is also requested to pay attention to the system of joint sanctions against recalcitrant aggressor countries as stated in the Covenant. Is there still any doubt that Japan is illegally engaging in war? In the face of this grave situation, only by acting quickly in accordance with the Covenant and implementing sanctions can the world know that the League of Nations values fairness and earnestly fulfills its supreme mission. What is this mission? It is international peace. After Dr. Gu finished speaking, Chairman Hymans asked if anyone else wished to speak. No one responded, so the Chairman announced the end of the discussion. The Chairman also stated that if no one opposed the resolution he had proposed, it would be considered passed. With no dissent, the resolution was declared passed, and the Assembly adjourned. (Reuters telegram, 24th)

Statement by the Chinese Embassy in London Regarding the Arms Embargo

China and Japan Should Not Be Treated Equally

(London) The Chinese Embassy issued the following statement: [In the military actions in Rehe, the Chinese side is engaged in legitimate self-defense, while Japan is engaged in a war of aggression. Therefore, the ban on the transportation of military arms and weapons, if applied equally to China and Japan, is not only unfair to China, but also practically amounts to favoring Japan, since Japan is already fully armed, while China is not.] [Havas telegram, 25th]

Future Work of the League of Nations

Significance of Representative Yan's Statement

(Nanjing) According to diplomatic sources, the League of Nations passed the report on the 24th, and we also voted in favor. However, Representative Yan stated that if Japan does not accept it, our country will not be affected at all. The meaning of Yan's statement is that in terms of obligations, if Japan does not fulfill the obligations of the proposed portion, we will not fulfill our obligations either. In terms of rights, if we accept the report, we will enjoy the stipulated rights, and other countries will not be allowed to declare war on us. Representative Gu raised the issue of Rehe at the Assembly, which was a preemptive move to leave room for invoking Article 16. The international community hopes that we will resist vigorously in Rehe. Now that the Assembly has passed the report, it will begin to implement the proposed portions one by one. The League of Nations will first establish an advisory committee, with the same tasks as the Special Committee of Nineteen, and will add Canada and the Netherlands, and invite the United States and Russia to strengthen its power. The Negotiation Committee will also be organized as soon as possible to report the results of the negotiations to the Assembly within three months. Therefore, the next three months are extremely important. Whether Japan will withdraw from the League of Nations is still uncertain, but it has no legal impact. The Advisory and Negotiation Committees can still carry out their work. (Central News Agency telegram, 25th)

Observations of Our Diplomats

Japan's Head-on Collision with the League of Nations

The Gains and Losses of Military Affairs Are of Great Importance

If We Can Resist for a Long Time, They Will Inevitably Fall into Chaos

(Nanjing) A key figure in diplomatic circles told reporters today that the spirit of the League of Nations' passage of the report is commendable, and its significance is also significant. Before the report was passed, the Sino-Japanese dispute could only be regarded as a dispute between two countries. After the report was passed, legally speaking, it has become a dispute between Japan and the League of Nations. In the next three months, the situation will become more serious, because Japan is extremely stubborn, and the League of Nations will exert its great power to bring Japan to justice. This is a major key to resolving the dispute. We are neither pessimistic nor disappointed, nor do we feel overjoyed. We only approach it with calmness. The situation in Rehe will expand due to Japan's stubbornness, and the gains and losses of military affairs are of great importance to diplomacy. We hope that the people and soldiers on the front lines will provide assistance in terms of spirit and materials. After the report was passed, Japan's diplomacy has fallen into a desperate situation, and its domestic economy is also in extreme panic. Stock prices have fallen by 900 million in a week. The military controls politics, and the cabinet is in a precarious state. If we can resist for a long time, they will inevitably fall into chaos. The most noteworthy thing is that Japan's aggressive militarism still does not dare to bear the responsibility for starting the war, and it is using all kinds of vicious schemes to shift the blame to us in order to resolve its domestic instability. We hope that the people will pay attention to this. (Central News Agency telegram, 25th)

Various Small Countries Support Our Withdrawal of the Envoy to Japan

(Nanjing) Yesterday, a telegram from Geneva relayed that our delegation suggested to the government to withdraw the envoy to Japan. According to reliable sources, the telegram has arrived in Beijing. The content is that the representatives of various small countries support our withdrawal of the envoy to Japan. Our delegation reported this to the government based on this telegram, and it was not a suggestion from the delegation. The diplomatic authorities seem to have considered this, but they refuse to express any opinion before a decision is made. (Central News Agency telegram, 25th)

Japan's Only Confidant

The World Is Big, But Only Siam Understands

Japanese Warlords Are Overwhelmed with Gratitude

(Tokyo) The Ministry of the Army of Japan heard that the Siamese representative abstained from voting at the League of Nations Assembly. The Army believes that Siam is its only confidant in the world. Today, it specially dispatched Colonel Honma, the head of the Army Press Corps, to visit the Siamese Embassy in Tokyo to express gratitude. It is reported that the Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs has also telegraphed Secretary-General Sawada to thank the Siamese representative in Geneva. (China United Press telegram, 25th)

U.S.-Japan War

The New York Times Believes It Is Impossible

Samoa Island Remains Under Military Control

(Washington) A Washington correspondent of the New York Times discussed the development of the Far East, saying that he had not met a responsible person who believed that there was a possibility of war between the United States and Japan, even in the distant future. (Reuters telegram, 25th) (Washington) Samoa Island in the South Pacific of the United States has always been under the administration of the Navy Department. The islanders requested to change to a civilian government. After Congress sent personnel to investigate in 1930, the Senate has passed a bill allowing the island to be governed by civilians. Today, it was suddenly rejected in the House of Representatives by a vote of 72 to 26. Although the island is in the Southwest Pacific, far from the islands under Japanese mandate, it is an important coal depot for the Navy. It occupies a strategic position militarily. With the situation in the Pacific becoming increasingly urgent, the U.S. Congress still wants to keep it under military control. (National News Agency telegram, 24th)

Page 8

League of Nations Report

U.S. Government Expresses Satisfaction

New Secretary of State Firmly States Support for Treaties

Hull Consults with Stimson on League of Nations Response

(Washington) U.S. government officials, while pleased with the League of Nations Assembly's adoption of the report drafted by the Committee of Nineteen, do not wish to make a public statement expressing their opinions, so as not to improperly increase the reaction of the public in various parts of the Far East. However, it is also being made known that these officials believe that the actions of the League of Nations are tantamount to realizing the United States' advocacy of maintaining treaties and not recognizing land acquired by force, and that it is also clear evidence that world opinion is solidified and supports the principles declared by the United States long ago. However, U.S. government officials feel that the situation is too serious, so they cannot hope that the United States will formally declare its reaction to the actions of the League of Nations early, and that since the change of government is less than two weeks away, any formal comment will have to wait for the new president. This is another reason why the U.S. government is not immediately expressing its opinion on the report. Although, U.S. official circles now expect the League of Nations to formally notify them of its report, at which time the United States will need to respond. It is expected that the U.S. government will express its satisfaction in the reply, because the League of Nations resolution is the same as the U.S. position. If this reply is issued before the change of government on March 4, it will be drafted by the future Secretary of State Hull in consultation with the State Council. It is reported that Hull will meet with Stimson for several hours tomorrow, and the discussion will focus on the entire diplomatic situation, with particular emphasis on the diplomacy of the Far East. Hull has always remained silent on the Manchurian issue, but Democratic leaders believe that he will adhere to the traditional U.S. policy. Furthermore, key Democratic figures say that the U.S. government will wait until the new government takes office before making a formal comment, and that this does not mean that there has been any change in policy, but rather that it is respecting the spirit of the new amendment to the Constitution, which stipulates that the change of the President and Cabinet will be changed from March 4 to early January. (National News Agency telegram, 24th)

(Washington) Mr. Hull, who was appointed Secretary of State by Roosevelt a few days ago, explained the future policy of the new U.S. government today. Hull told guests that the United States should pay attention to the words and spirit of any other country's compliance with treaties and international contracts, without allowing any slack. At the same time, there must also be sound and practical international cooperation to help maintain world peace, while not forgetting the habits of the United States and the Constitution of the United States. The success of the new government's foreign policy will depend on the extent to which the United States helps restore world commerce and maintain world peace. (Reuters telegram, 24th)

Japan Hesitates on the Issue of Withdrawing from the League of Nations

Emergency Cabinet Meeting Ends Without Result

Uchida Again Visits the Emperor

(Tokyo) Before the extraordinary cabinet meeting opened at 2:30 p.m. today, Foreign Minister Uchida entered the palace to visit the Emperor, reporting on the proceedings of yesterday's League of Nations Assembly. He left after about half an hour.

(Tokyo) An emergency cabinet meeting was held at the Prime Minister's residence at 4 p.m. today. After Foreign Minister Uchida reported on the League of Nations proceedings, he introduced the situation of various countries toward Japan. Army Minister Araki continued to report on the situation in Rehe. However, regarding the withdrawal from the League of Nations, it was originally scheduled to be decided at today's cabinet meeting, and the procedure for consulting the Privy Council would be taken immediately. Because the official report from the delegation has not yet arrived, only the situation was reported today. After the official report arrives, it will be decided at the extraordinary cabinet meeting on the 27th. (Electric News telegram, 25th)

(Tokyo) Yesterday, the Assembly passed a proposed resolution, and the attitude of the League of Nations has reached its final decision. The Japanese government convened an emergency cabinet meeting today to formally decide on the withdrawal policy, and immediately issued a major instruction to the delegation to withdraw. However, the procedures for the abrogation of the Treaty of Versailles require consultation with the Privy Council. After the cabinet meeting, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and the Bureau of Legislation began to prepare everything. (Electric News Agency telegram, 25th)

(Geneva) With the League of Nations Assembly coming to an end, the Japanese delegation has decided to withdraw from Geneva. Representative Matsuoka is scheduled to leave Geneva for Paris at 2:30 p.m. on the 25th. Representative Nagaoka is scheduled to leave for Paris at 9:40 p.m. on the same day. Representative Sato is scheduled to leave for Brussels on the 28th. (Electric News Agency telegram, 24th)

(Geneva) According to official claims from the Japanese side, Japan will at least temporarily not withdraw its representatives from the Disarmament Conference. Even if the Japanese government is forced to withdraw from the League of Nations, it will continue to cooperate with other major powers so that the disarmament plan can be resolved. (National News Agency telegram, 25th)

(Geneva) The League of Nations has not yet been able to fully believe that Japan will actually withdraw from the League of Nations. It is said that Japan may take the attitude of an outsider, ignoring all League of Nations resolutions, and only send an observer to participate informally, as the United States does, when meetings are held. (National News Agency telegram, 24th)

are greatly surprised by the news from Geneva that Japan intends to negotiate and conclude a non-aggression treaty with the Dutch government, including the Dutch East Indies. A Glimpse of Public Opinion in Various Countries

Banning the Supply of Arms and Money to Japan

The Theory of Taking International Action Is Gaining Strength

(New York) The New York Times said that the League of Nations' unanimous resolution against Japan's actions is extremely important. Even if Japan leaves the League of Nations, it will eventually not escape the condemnation of conscience. Whether Japan is in or out of the League, this morally important judgment will eventually make Japan uneasy. The New York World-Telegram said that the League of Nations has been established for fourteen years, and it is only now that it has a clear position. The future of the League of Nations depends on the future of the Far Eastern issue. If moral condemnation and non-recognition are still ineffective, then peace-loving people will inevitably find another way to solve this difficult problem. (Reuters telegram, 25th)

(London) The Manchester Guardian said in today's society column that the League of Nations Assembly's passage of the report of the Special Committee of Nineteen is a victory over itself, not a victory over Japan. However, it will have to defeat Japan in the future. Any country that accepts the League of Nations' verdict cannot sell arms to Japan, otherwise it will be an accomplice to the barbaric war that violates the treaty. (Reuters telegram, 25th)

(London) The Times published an editorial today, saying that there are various reasons why it is extremely desirable for Japan to maintain its cooperation with the Disarmament Conference. A major power like Japan would never deign to completely refuse to participate in the good work that the League of Nations has painstakingly managed simply because its opinion on a dispute differs from that of the League of Nations. The newspaper continued, saying that Matsuoka's statement that "we are willing to assist China" need not be doubted. It is by no means impossible for Japan to temporarily apply a better administration to Manchuria. Then, the result of its current actions may allow parts of North China to enjoy security and peace. Japan claims that it is now engaged in the work of civilization, and its words are not unreasonable, but its breach of promise and its denial of treaties and various obligations under the League of Nations Covenant are undeniable. Since the methods of the Japanese warlords cannot be compatible with the principles of the League of Nations, the League of Nations has no other way but to refute such methods. Although the League of Nations' position cannot force the implementation of the agreed solution, the member states are responsible for doing their best to achieve the final victory. Their clear responsibility today is not to assist in any way countries that seek to impose their own solutions by force. The Times concluded that, in the months before the dispute, at least export licenses should not be issued for any arms and ammunition shipped to Japan. (Reuters telegram, 25th) (London) Today, all the London morning newspapers used Japan and the League of Nations as the main material for their commentaries. The News Chronicle said that countries should immediately implement international action to ban the supply of arms and money to Japan. The definition of "contraband" by the British Admiralty during World War I can be reinstated. The Daily Express said that any resolution on matters of great importance to Great Britain and the Empire should be issued in London, not in Geneva. The Daily Mirror said urgently that we should be careful to look far ahead, refuse to go to war, and not hold the empty hope of stopping the war others are brewing. The Daily Mail said that from today onwards, the League of Nations or any member state of the League of Nations cannot claim to be completely neutral in honor or responsibility. China should at least receive the spiritual assistance of any country that upholds the League of Nations Covenant. (Reuters telegram, 25th)

(Paris) Today, French newspapers thoroughly discussed the dramatic posture of the Japanese representative's work in Geneva yesterday, and what important impact it will have on the League of Nations. The newspapers believe that the Eastern island nation will now withdraw from the League of Nations. The left-wing newspapers still resent Japan, saying that the League of Nations has exhausted its ability to prevent Japan from expanding its imperialism in the war in Rehe. The right-wing newspapers said that Japan has tolled the funeral bell for the League of Nations. The League of Nations can do nothing more than organize a committee to send personnel to monitor developments. It is a big mistake for the League of Nations to exclude Japan. (Reuters telegram, 25th) (Paris) French political circles are paying close attention to the severity of the situation in Geneva and Rehe. The government is closely monitoring current events. It is reported that it is opposed to any form of sanctions against Japan. The Times reported that the real Sino-Japanese war has only just begun, and the only hope is for China and Japan to find a solution before the war extends into North China. The Debats reported that if the Japanese army invades the Chinese mainland, it is feared that there will be a very serious dispute, which will lead to foreign intervention. The Paris Evening Post exclusively urged the League of Nations to implement economic sanctions. The Liberté believes that the League of Nations has intentionally or unintentionally succumbed to the influence of the United States, isolating Japan. (Reuters telegram, 25th)

Japanese Troops in Tianjin Create a Terrifying Situation

Installing Iron Fences, Laying Electric Nets, Stacking Sandbags

Armed Japanese Soldiers Guarding at the Border

Women Willing to Take on Work and Join Hospitals to Practice First Aid

(Tianjin) The enemy has plans to disturb Beiping and Tianjin, and our authorities have stepped up preparations and strengthened the rear defense. Japanese troops stationed in Tianjin have installed iron fences at the Sino-Japanese border, a total of eleven, ostensibly to prevent bandits, but actually military defense works. In an emergency, electricity will be turned on to replace the electric nets. On the morning of the 25th, Japanese soldiers installed electric nets and stacked sandbags in the area from the Wall River to the Haiguang Temple Japanese barracks. The electric nets are taller and stronger than those during the Tianjin Incident the year before last. (Special telegram, 25th)

When necessary, all Sino-Japanese crossings will be closed. (Special telegram, 25th)

(Tianjin) Japanese women and children in Tianjin are unwilling to return to their country and are willing to serve the Japanese army, which has been understood by Nakamura. They are now in charge of sewing hemp bags, making electric nets, and stacking sandbags. On the 25th, Japanese women also worked to install iron fences at the Sino-Japanese crossings. Another group of Japanese women were sent to various hospitals to practice nursing and first aid. From 6 p.m. on the evening of the 25th, fully armed Japanese soldiers were stationed at the Sino-Japanese crossings, facing our police posts from a distance. The Japanese consulate, the Japanese police station, and the Japanese barracks are all stocked with sandbags, laid with electric nets, and heavily guarded. (Special telegram, 25th)

Constitutional Drafting Committee Decides on the Elements of a Nation

Appointment of Research Committee Members for Each Group

(Nanjing) The Constitutional Draft Committee has tentatively made the following decisions regarding the research on the elements of the state: 1. Territory: Enumeration of provinces and regions; 2. Form of Government: The Republic of China is a Republic based on the Three Principles of the People; 3. Sovereignty: Belongs to the citizens of the Republic of China; 4. Flag Color: Remains the same (i.e., Blue Sky, White Sun, and a Red Earth). These will be submitted to the constitutional draft on March 2nd. (Central News Agency dispatch, 25th)

(Nanjing) The Legislative Yuan has appointed members to the Constitutional Draft Committee to conduct group research. Group 1: Territory, Form of Government, Sovereignty, Flag Color Committee: Wu Jingxiong and six others, convener Zhang Zhiben. Group 2: Rights and Obligations of the People, People's Livelihood Committee: Ma Yinchu and ten others, convener Wu Jingxiong. Group 3: National Diplomacy, Exercise of Four Powers, Committee on Equal Distribution of Power between the Central and Local Governments: Jiao Yitang and ten others, convener Zhang Zhiben. Group 4: Central Government System, Provincial System, County System Committee: Ding Chaowu and ten others, convener Chuan Bingchang. (Central News Agency dispatch, 25th)

(Nanjing) Zhang Zhiben, Deputy Chairman of the Constitution Drafting Committee, said: Regarding the territorial issue in the draft constitution, I believe that enumeration is advisable. Because our country is surrounded by powerful nations, border negotiations are sometimes unavoidable. If the territory is not defined by enumeration, it will easily provoke the expansionist ambitions of the other party. This is clearly demonstrated by the various fabrications that the violent Japanese made to the League of Nations when they invaded and occupied the Northeast. Looking at the territorial provisions in the constitutions of modern Austria and Mexico, their intentions are exactly the same. The drafting of a written constitution does not shy away from being detailed. The so-called enumeration is to list the names of each province, as well as Mongolia, Tibet, and various special regions, clearly indicating the scope of the territory, in order to prevent the covetousness of powerful neighbors. Colleagues all agree with this opinion and will draft according to this principle in the future. (Special dispatch, 25th)

[P Heavy Snow Suddenly Fell in the Capital

Spherical Hailstones Fell to the Ground with a Sound

(Nanjing) Heavy snow suddenly fell at around 5 p.m. The hailstones were spherical, larger than beans, and fell to the ground with a sound. It lasted for about 20 minutes, but it was only in the southern part of the city and was not widespread. (Special dispatch, 25th)

(Nanjing) After February 23rd, the temperature in the capital suddenly dropped sharply, especially on the 25th, with almost every drop of water turning into ice. According to the Meteorological Research Institute, the average climate this year is slightly colder than last year. The temperature gradually increased on February 19th and 20th, reaching 17.3 degrees Celsius on the 21st, which was the highest temperature since the beginning of spring. This was because the Siberian cold air had not come south, and the southern warm air had moved north. Until 6 p.m. on the 23rd, the wind direction turned from south to north very strongly, and the cold air arrived here, so the recent days have been in a cold air state. On the 25th, the temperature dropped to minus 2.8 degrees Celsius, but the cold air is now moving eastward, and the climate in the capital will soon warm up. (Central News Agency dispatch, 25th)

One Wave Subsides, Another Rises: American Financial Turmoil

Two Hundred and Five Banks in Maryland Suspend Operations

(Reuters, Baltimore, 24th) Today, the Governor of Maryland, Ritchie, ordered all banks within the state to temporarily close until next Wednesday to avoid losses to both banks and depositors after a run on deposits. Currently, a total of 205 banks have suspended operations throughout the state. Over the past week, depositors have been withdrawing funds. Apart from ordinary commercial transactions and ordinary payments, withdrawals throughout the state have exceeded 13 million yuan. This morning, for some unknown reason, there was a large-scale run on banks. Two of them will be unable to open tomorrow. The governor urgently summoned a meeting of the state's six major banks and then issued an order for all of them to suspend operations, shocking the nation. However, according to the governor, all banks in the state have a solid foundation, and only a few cannot cope with the sudden run. Currently, the state legislature is considering a bill to limit the amount of withdrawals that depositors can make without prior notice. Now that a financial crisis has occurred, both houses will quickly pass this bill, and it is expected that the governor will sign it into law on Tuesday.

(Reuters, Lansing, 24th) The difficult problem caused by the bank holiday in Michigan has now been resolved. It can be implemented after the Currency Administrator in Washington approves it. This plan advocates organizing two new banks to receive the liquid assets of the two largest banks in Detroit.

Hitler's Dictatorship

National Socialist Stormtroopers Obtain Police Powers Berlin Dispatch from the 24th: German Chancellor Hitler, in terms of maintaining order, can now practically be called a dictator. This is because the government has granted police powers to the National Socialist Stormtroopers under his command. Meanwhile, Goering, the administrative commissioner in charge of Prussian police affairs, also stated that the Prussian police will fully cooperate with the National Socialist Stormtroopers to maintain local order. Furthermore, strong and sturdy individuals will be selected from the Stormtroopers and the Steel Helmet organization to form police auxiliary teams, wearing special armbands and led by formal police officers. Their main task is to protect election campaigns and public utilities and buildings when disturbances occur during meetings. As for the reason why the government granted police powers to the Stormtroopers, it is said that the current police force is too weak to cope with the increasing number of emergencies and violations of the law, as well as the attacks by the Communist Party. Berlin Dispatch from the 24th: With the date of the German parliamentary re-election approaching, all the people in the country are eager to know the only big question: if this re-election still fails to secure a majority of the pro-government faction in the new parliament, what changes will occur in the situation afterwards? The leaders of the pro-government faction seem to have a clear plan for this question and have revealed it slightly in previous election campaign speeches. Among the most important ones, Chancellor Hitler has clearly stated that March 5th is the only opportunity for the German people to voluntarily entrust the future of the country to the current government. However, if the German people do not release this right path, the current government cannot allow the country to be taken over by the parties that will destroy the nation, and take themselves to destruction. This view is the same as that of Steel Helmet leader and Minister of National Defense Seld. It is said that the life of the current government will definitely not be limited to March 5th, but will be extended for several years until it can successfully guide the people of the whole country and obtain their approval. As for the opposition's arguments, they are still trying their best to oppose the government with a small majority and say that the current government will definitely not have the opportunity to obtain a majority in the next parliament.

League of Nations Handles Colombian-Peruvian Dispute

Unusual Negotiation Conditions

Geneva Dispatch from Havas News Agency on the 25th: This agency's correspondent in Geneva has learned that the Executive Council of the League of Nations has organized a committee. This committee, representing the Executive Council, notified the Peruvian government of the basic conditions for beneficial negotiations to resolve the dispute between Peru and Colombia. The conditions are as follows: (1) The negotiations should be based on the recognition of Colombia's sovereignty in Leticia; (2) Leticia should be an international city, administered by the Colombian government under the commission of the International League. Colombia seems to have accepted the internationalization of Leticia, but the Peruvian government is trying to revise the Salomón-Lozano Treaty, because according to that treaty, the disputed area is to be governed by Colombia.

Overview of the Japanese Attack on Rehe

It is a gift from heaven, a virgin land,

And we must not allow it to be seized by the Japanese.

But the Japanese shout to raise the axe of reclamation,

The sooner the better, to hack into Rehe.

Since the fall of Shanhaiguan, the Rehe issue has become a stimulant for Japanese warlords to take another step on the foothold of militarism. At the same time, it has also become a touchstone for our country's authorities to "resist humiliation with strength and resist for a long time." In order to make the people of the country understand the truth about the Rehe issue, the following is a brief description of the general situation of Rehe.

Territory

Rehe includes the Zhaowuda League and Zhuosotu League in eastern Inner Mongolia, and the Mulan Paddock, which was a hunting ground for the emperor during the Qing Dynasty. The provincial boundary stretches from 40 degrees to 46 degrees north latitude and from 116 degrees to 122 degrees east longitude, with a total area of approximately 580,000 square miles. It is backed by the Greater Khingan Mountains, which meander from northeast to southwest. To the west is the Yinshan Mountains, which run from the Helan Mountains around the north side of the Hetao area, across the provinces of Suiyuan and Chahar to Baicha Mountain. The northeastern branch is the dividing line between Rehe and Chahar, and the southern branch winds through Rehe, forming the Qilaotu Mountains and the Nuluerhuling Mountains. There are also the Songling Mountains, which run parallel to the Bohai coast and serve as a barrier to the southeastern border of Rehe. The northeast borders Liaoning Province, stretching thousands of miles and forming a very large plain. The northern part is undulating hills, the southeast is a plain, and the central and southern parts have rivers and high mountains intertwined. The rivers include the Luan River, the Daling River, and the Xiaoling River.

People

Rehe was originally part of Inner Mongolia. During the Qianlong period of the Qing Dynasty, Shandong and Zhili (now Hebei) provinces were overcrowded, and the people had no way to make a living, so they moved here in droves. The residents of Rehe counties today are mostly descendants of people who moved from Shandong and Zhili provinces. Their clothing, food, housing, and daily habits are no different from those of residents within the customs. However, there are still a small number of Mongolians living on the wastelands in the western and northeastern parts, living a nomadic life of following the water and grass. Rehe has a population of about four or five million, almost entirely Han Chinese. Mongolians and Manchus account for only a very small number.

Climate

The climate of Rehe is quite inconsistent due to the complexity of the mountains and rivers in the territory. Generally, because it is farther away from the ocean, it has the characteristics of a continental climate. In terms of climate, each year can be divided into four seasons. Spring lasts about one month (from early May to early June), summer lasts about two months (from mid-June to early August), autumn lasts about one month (from early August to early September), and the remaining seven or eight months are all winter. The hottest month of the year is July, with a maximum temperature of 60 degrees Celsius, and the coldest month is January, with a minimum temperature dropping to minus 30 degrees Celsius. However, because the climate is continental, the rainfall is extremely low. The number of rainy days throughout the year is only about 20 days, and the rainfall is also very unevenly distributed. The months with the most rainfall in a year are between June and August, but most of them are showers and light rain, lasting only a few hours at a minimum and no more than one or two days at most. Because there are very few trees, the rivers are very prone to flooding. Traffic is often blocked after each rainfall. There is also very little snow, only about four or five times a year. If the climate changes drastically, it often snows in May, and the rivers begin to freeze in October, not melting until early April of the following year. However, due to the different climates in the north and south, the period of freezing and thawing is also slightly different. The north is windy throughout the year, especially in spring and winter. The wind is quite strong. From May to September, the winds are mostly southerly, or southeasterly and southwesterly. From October onwards, the wind is severe, piercing the skin, and is northwesterly.

Products

Rehe is endowed with rich natural resources,

Extremely rich, which is coveted by the Japanese. The following is a general description of its products:

Rice: Approximately 45,000 stones

Wheat: Approximately 400,000 stones

Sorghum: Approximately 1,500,000 stones

Wool: Approximately 2,000,000 stones

As for minerals, coal is produced in Xinqiu, Daninggou, Yuejiagou, Xiyuanbaoshan, Shidafen, Wujia, Songshutai, and other places. In addition, wool, licorice, and other various medicinal materials are also special products of Rehe, and the annual output is also quite considerable.

In summary, it can be seen that Rehe is indeed a divinely blessed country, a virgin land. Whether from a political or economic point of view, Rehe must not be seized by the Japanese. Currently, the Japanese are all frantically shouting [Hurry up and raise the axe of reclamation, the sooner the better, to hack into Rehe], and the total mobilization for aggression against us has also begun. Then, what should we do? I hope all the people of the country will think about it.

The Communist Suppression in Jiangxi Province Is About to Launch a General Attack

The Joint Suppression by the Armies of Four Provinces Is Complete; Party and Government Personnel and the Masses Are Mobilized

Nanchang Correspondence: After Chairman Chiang arrived in Jiangxi, he actively deployed the Communist suppression campaign. He considered both military, political, and party affairs, and also made thorough arrangements on the borders of Jiangxi, Guangdong, Fujian, Zhejiang, Hunan, and Hubei provinces. It is reported that the date of the general attack is not far away. The following is a record of important news about the Communist suppression:

Military Affairs

In the past two large-scale encirclement and suppression campaigns, the military aspect focused solely on Jiangxi, where the Red Army was located. The regions bordering Jiangxi, though nominally involved in the joint suppression, were in fact watching each other from across the border, allowing Zhu De and Mao Zedong to calmly flee to Guangdong and Fujian, nurturing the wound and causing harm, leading to today's mobilization of two or three hundred thousand troops, wasting the anti-Japanese forces. Therefore, before this suppression campaign, Chiang, in addition to sending Huang Shaohong to Guangdong to request that Guangdong and Guangxi send troops to Jiangxi to assist in the suppression, also transferred a certain unit from Zhejiang to Jiangxi, to cooperate with the Guangdong army. At the same time, he ordered the various divisions in western Fujian and the armies on the Fu River in eastern Jiangxi to attack from both sides, so that the Zhu Mao forces in the border areas of Jiangxi, Guangdong, Fujian, and Zhejiang could be surrounded on all sides, making it impossible for them to escape. Only in this way can their main force be identified, so as to avoid the situation where the bandits come when the troops leave, and the bandits leave when the troops come. As for the joint suppression by the armies of the four provinces, in addition to gradually taking a defensive posture, the other three provinces all took an offensive posture. (A) Jiangxi is the center of the Communist suppression, with a military force of more than 200,000, of which at least more than 100,000 are assigned to eastern Jiangxi. Chiang has appointed Chen Cheng, the commander of the Fu River front, as the commander-in-chief of the Central Route Army, with three columns under his command. It is said that Chen Cheng, the commander of the 18th Army, Luo Zhuoying, the commander of the 5th Army, and Wu Qiwu, the commander of the 4th Army, will be appointed as the commanders of the first, second, and third columns, respectively. The armies and divisions in eastern Jiangxi all belong to it and are generally controlled by Chen Cheng. They will advance towards the border in three routes, and will recover Jinxi, Zixi, Lichuan, and Guangchang in the shortest possible time, and then join forces with the Guangdong and Fujian armies to attack Ruijin and Ningdu. Chen assumed the position of commander-in-chief of the Central Route on the 12th in the province, and the commanders of each column also reported to the capital to take office. Chen has been discussing military plans with Chiang in the province for days, mobilizing border troops, and distributing forces. As soon as everything is ready, he will rush to the front to issue a general attack order. (B) The northeastern border of Guangdong is intertwined with the borders of Jiangxi and Fujian. It is reported that Chen Jitang sent Yang Dezhao as a representative to Jiangxi to meet Chiang and discuss the issue of Guangdong and Guangxi sending troops. Yang stayed in the province for a week, and a proper plan has been discussed in military terms. Chiang also agreed to provide financial assistance. Yang took the satisfactory contact and left for Xun on the night of the 14th with Li Shangyong, the representative of the 8th Route Army stationed in Jiangxi, and then returned to Guangdong via Shanghai to report to Chen. Recently, the headquarters has received telegrams from Chen Jitang and Li Zongren, expressing their agreement with the military plan brought back by Yang. Chiang also appointed Yu Hanmou as the commander-in-chief of the Left Route Army, leading the Guangdong and Guangxi armies from Ganzhou, Anyuan, and Huichang to Xingguo and Yudu, with the goal of attacking Ruijin, where the false central government is located. (C) On the Fujian side, Chiang appointed Cai Tingkai as the commander-in-chief of the Left Route Army on the 14th, and all units in Fujian were under his control. Cai telegraphed Chiang on the 16th, saying that he had taken office in Fuzhou, and immediately ordered all of them to mobilize and advance towards the Jiangxi border.

Party and Government

Chiang considered Communist suppression as treating the symptoms with military force and treating the root cause with party and government affairs. Regarding the aftermath of the bandit areas, the post-disaster committee jointly formed by the military, government, and party was in charge. Chiang also appointed Chen Cheng as the chairman of the committee, with two offices under his command: party affairs and government affairs. Gong Boxun, a member of the provincial government, served as the director of the government affairs office, and Li Zhongxiang, a member of the provincial reorganization committee, served as the director of the party affairs office. They were ordered by the chairman to handle all party and government affairs in the recovered areas, handle the aftermath, and were no different from a battlefield government affairs meeting. Gong Boxun reported to take office on the 17th, organized road construction teams, captured bandit receiving teams, etc., to build roads with the army and take charge of military transportation. In the bandit-occupied counties, Ningdu, Ruijin, Shicheng, Guangchang, Yudu, Huichang, Anyuan, Xunwu, and Lichuan were set up as eight post-disaster groups in order to clean up the remnants, handle rescue and healing, restore order, and recruit refugees when they were captured.

Masses

All sectors of the province unanimously participated in the Communist suppression. Therefore, after Chiang's visit to Jiangxi, a mass assistance committee for Communist suppression was established in Nanchang, with branches set up in all counties that had not been captured by the bandits and in all villages and towns near the bandit areas. According to the committee's plan: (1) Organize an economic committee to raise funds to help the army and provide disaster relief. (2) Organize a 15,000-member iron shoulder team to take charge of military transportation. (3) All vocational groups will set up a coordination association to lead their members to do their best in manpower and financial resources to carry out the general mobilization of the Communist suppression work. (4) Make widespread publicity and movement, and strictly implement frugality this year, unite and rise up to help complete the Communist suppression work. The remaining items are all in progress.

Bandit Situation

The Red Army in this province originally had Zhu, Mao, Peng, Fang, Shao, Kong Hechong, Li Tianzhu, and other factions. Fang and Shao have already fled from northeastern Jiangxi to southern Xinjiang in eastern Jiangxi and joined forces with Zhu and Mao. Only a part of the remnant bandits are still in the old Guangxin territory north of Xinjiang, including Hengtiao, Yiyang, Wannian, Guixi, and Yujiang. They are now being jointly suppressed by the divisions stationed in Zhejiang, Anhui, and northeastern Jiangxi. Kong Hechong's pseudo-16th Army, except for the 9th Division that fled back to southern Hubei, the pseudo-7th and 8th Divisions, the pseudo-Independent 1st, 2nd, and 3rd Divisions, and the pseudo-Red Police Division, are still scattered in the border area of the three provinces of Xiushui, Ganggu, and Wanzai. They are now being jointly suppressed by the divisions under the command of Zhu Shaoliang. Li Tianzhu's pseudo-8th Army was formed by gathering scattered bandits from western Jiangxi and the Hunan border. Yongxin and Ninggang were used as bases, and they emerged in the areas of Wan'an, Taihe, Suichuan, Lianhua, Anfu, Chongyi, and Shangyou. It is reported that the Hunan army has actually entered Jiangxi and joined forces with the Guangdong army in Chongyou and the certain divisions in Suichuan and Taihe. As for Zhu, Mao, Peng, and others, they are not only the leaders of the bandits, but also the leaders of the largest Red Army in the country. Their pseudo-central government is located in Ruijin, and only a small number of pseudo-student soldiers, guards divisions, and replenishment divisions are stationed there. Their main force is following Zhu and Mao to commit crimes in the border areas of Fujian and Jiangxi. Their pseudo-1st, 3rd, and 5th Army Groups, the pseudo-22nd Army, six pseudo-Independent Divisions, and Fang Shao's pseudo-10th Army, totaling about 40,000 to 50,000 people with 20,000 to 30,000 guns, are entrenched from the Guangdong border in the south, through northwestern Fujian, southeastern Jiangxi, to the border between western Zhejiang and eastern Jiangxi. The main force of this group originally fled to the Zhejiang border, but recently suddenly moved south, concentrating its main force in Lichuan and Zixi. On the one hand, the pseudo-3rd and 5th Army Groups besieged Nanfeng, and on the other hand, the pseudo-1st Army Group fled back to Jinxi from Zixi, and at the same time, the pseudo-4th and 5th Independent Divisions attacked Yihuang, attempting to make a final gamble, but they were all defeated by various armies. Once the general attack of the four provinces' armies is launched, it should not be difficult to completely wipe them out.

The Rampancy of Local Bandits in Northern Hubei

The bandits have a total of nine divisions, with a crowd of ten thousand people. The counties of Suizao have been robbed severely. The Luo Brigade is advancing to suppress the bandits in Henan territory. Hankou Correspondence: Since the major groups of Red Army bandits in Hubei Province gradually died out, the survivors in the bandit areas seemed to have hope for recuperation, but the local bandits in various places have not been eliminated, so their power has gradually increased. For example, a large group of local bandits was recently discovered in Sanhe Village, which belongs to Suixian County in northern Hubei, totaling about four or five thousand people, formed by the union of various groups from Henan, Hubei, and Shaanxi. The bandits call the bandit groups "divisions," and the bandit leaders are called "division leaders." For example, the group formed by the Zhang family is called the Zhang Division, and the group formed by the Yang family is called the Yang Division. They used to harass the counties of Sui, Zao, and Zhongxiang. The bandits include the Zhang, Yang, Gu, Ma, Mao, and Liu Divisions, and Zhang and Yang actually hold the key to the whole group, like the alliance leader among the chieftains, because their followers are more numerous and their weapons are more sophisticated. The Zhang bandit's name is Ruiwu, and the Yang bandit's name is unknown. They are rebel soldiers from a certain unit in Shaanxi Province. The banner reads the First Security Regiment. Zhang and Yang both claim to be regimental commanders, with more than two thousand people, complete equipment, and mortars and machine guns. The bandits mostly speak with a Henan and Shaanxi accent. After entering Hubei territory, the leaders of the Gu Desheng, Liu Xinghan, Chen Hanqing, and Mao Xing family's divisions successively joined them. The Gu, Liu, Chen, and Mao Divisions are local bandits in Zao Yang, who disturb the border of Sui Zhong. The number of people varies and the guns and bullets are not very complete. The bandits without guns are replaced by sticks to serve as "guides" and "ticket takers," because they are natives. As for the Ma Regiment, it fled from Yichang Jingmen, with no less than a thousand followers. On New Year's Eve, it fled to Sanhe Village and occupied it as its lair. The two divisions of Ze Tao Yu and Kang Cai Wu, who were originally stationed there, also joined forces, and their power became even greater. Pan's office has been defending the area for many years, and Kang used to be the head of the regiment of Fan Zhongxiu's department. It is incomprehensible that they are willing to join the bandits.

After Zhang and Yang's bandits entered Sui and Zao, every village and town they passed was looted. No less than a thousand people were kidnapped. For example, when the bandits first fled from Suiyang Inn, they fell into Zishan. All four hundred households in the city were looted. A Mr. Sun was brutally killed on the spot. It was in the middle of the night, and the residents were all asleep. The bandits kidnapped everyone, regardless of the poor or the rich, about five hundred people in total. After the bandit leaders interrogated them one by one, if a family was completely kidnapped, one person would be released to raise money to redeem the ticket. Those who were truly impoverished were released. In addition to those who were released, a total of more than two hundred and seventy people were kidnapped. Zishan originally belonged to the eastern second district of Zao. After the bandits robbed it, they went to the Liusong area in the southern third and fifth districts to harass. Then, they fell into the Fule River, which belongs to Zhongxiang, and robbed more than a thousand men and women. Then, they entrenched themselves in the Matou Village and Niutou Village north of the town, waiting for the ticket redemption. When the Ma Division came to meet from Jingyi, they turned north and fled to Bawan Mountain, Liangtan Pan, Shiyan Village, and Majia Village, where they searched and robbed extensively. Finally, they concentrated in Sanhe Village and sent their partisans to burn and kill in all directions. The victims are probably tens of thousands of families.

Feng's Faction Sends Xu Qian Southward

Representatives from Guizhou, Yunnan, and Hunan also Arrive in Guangzhou One After Another

Guangzhou Dispatch: Recently, representatives from various parties have been arriving in Guangzhou in a continuous stream. The most notable of these is Xu Qian, representing Feng Yuxiang. It is said that Xu has already arrived in Hong Kong, keeping his movements extremely secret. While in Hong Kong, he met with Hu Hanmin and Li Jishen. Xu's mission is approximately to report on the situation of Feng's old subordinates and to connect with the Southwest. Xu also mentioned that most of Feng Yuxiang's old subordinates are eager to serve the country, but they are facing economic difficulties. If the Southwest could provide assistance, they could rise up and become the vanguard against foreign aggression.

The Southwest Political Affairs Council has recently been focusing on uniting the various provinces in the Southwest. Previously, it dispatched Mai Huanzhang to Guiyang to coordinate everything. Now that the situation in Guizhou has stabilized somewhat, Mai has been further dispatched from Guizhou to Sichuan to contact a certain general in Sichuan. As for Wang Jialie of Guizhou Province, he recently sent Lu Shou to Guangzhou as his plenipotentiary representative and also sent Zhang Yunliang to Guangzhou to organize the Guizhou Army's office in Guangzhou. Wang also sent a telegram to Guangzhou yesterday, reporting that the Guizhou Army's Wu Jianping led the remnants of his troops to retreat to Xingren and requested reorganization. In order to clear the western routes and facilitate trade between Yunnan and Guizhou, Wang has ordered Commander Bai Huizhang to lead his troops across the river. Commander Bai's troops entered Xingren on the 13th, and the two battalions of Wu's troops, Zhou and Song, collapsed. Commander Bai dispatched teams to disarm and reorganize them. It is said that the western defense of Guizhou Province will be completed and stabilized within days. It is rumored that after the defeat of Mao Guangxiang, You Guocai, and others in Guizhou, they either went to Sichuan to request assistance or went to Beijing to ask for instructions. Therefore, the Southwest urgently dispatched Mai Huanzhang from Guizhou to Sichuan to discuss countermeasures with a certain Sichuan army general. Bai Chongxi of Guangxi Province also rushed back to Guangxi from Guangzhou in order to coordinate with Wang of Guizhou. Therefore, the war in Guizhou is not only an internal dispute but also an undercurrent of struggle between two major forces behind it. Regarding Yunnan's attitude, it previously sent representatives Dan Maoxin and Zhang Chong to Guangzhou. Zhang Chong soon left Guangzhou for Shanghai, but Dan remained in the province. According to Dan, this time he was ordered by Long (Yun) of Yunnan to discuss important political matters with the Guangxi authorities because there are many issues to be resolved due to the relationship between neighboring provinces. Therefore, he first went to Guangxi and then came to Guangzhou. It is premature to say that Yunnan has joined the Southwest National Defense Council. According to a message from the Political Affairs Council yesterday, after Dan arrived in Guangzhou and met with various officials, he telegraphed Long Yun on the 18th, reporting the results of the negotiations. Whether Yunnan will join the Southwest National Defense Council or not is still awaiting Long's reply.

He Jian of Hunan Province also sent representative Ling Zhang to the province on the 15th of this month to meet with military, political, and party leaders here. It is said that they are discussing issues such as suppressing the communists and resisting Japan. The Southwest Political Affairs Council also intends to send someone to Hunan in return. (February 19th)

Guangzhou Authorities Secretly Reject Li

Chen Hanyu's Murder is Related to the Rejection of Li; Li Jishen Sends Letters to Various Generals to Clarify Rumors

Guangzhou Dispatch: The military authorities in Guangdong Province recently suddenly executed Chen Hanyu, the former chief of staff of the Fourth Army Group. It is rumored that this is related to the rejection of Li Jishen's return to Guangdong. On the 12th of this month, Chen was residing in Dongshan when he was suddenly arrested by military police. On the 13th, he was sent to the military law office of the First Army Group Headquarters for interrogation. On the afternoon of the 13th, a team was sent to escort Chen to Honghuagang for execution. The headquarters also posted a notice near the execution ground, stating that retired soldier Chen Hanyu had been appearing in Guangzhou, plotting wrongdoing. After interrogation, he was found guilty and sentenced to death. Chen was originally the commander of the Fifth Army Corps. In 1924, he served in an important position in the General Headquarters and was appreciated by Sun Yat-sen. In 1931, when the new National Government was established in Guangzhou, a staff group was organized. At that time, Li Jishen's confidant Feng Zhuwan served as the director of the staff group, and Feng appointed Chen Hanyu as the deputy director of the staff group. It seems that Chen was close to Li Jishen. However, the Guangdong authorities have a very poor relationship with Li Jishen. When Li first went south to Hong Kong, the Guangdong authorities blocked him. Before long, Li's confidant Feng Zhuwan lost his position as director of the Department of Finance because of this matter. When Li recently went south to Hong Kong for the second time, the Guangdong authorities were on guard again, and it is not known how. There was suddenly a rumor that Li would be appointed chairman of the Southwest National Defense Council. The Guangdong authorities formally denied this and further tightened their guard against Li's activities. Chen Hanyu was arrested and executed at this time, so it is suspected that it is related to the prevention of Li. After Chen's death, the government's anti-Li propaganda became more intense, saying that Li had not made a clear handover when he left office in Guangdong and had recently sent a letter to Chen Bonan (Jitang), requesting funds for activities. Therefore, Li immediately sent a long letter to the generals in Guangdong from Hong Kong, stating that "Since I took office in the Fourth Army until the Eighth Route Army, one term replaced another. Brother Bonan took over the Fourth Army, and brother Bonan also happened to take over the Eighth Route Army, which your brothers can all remember. However, both times the handover was done by Ma Binghong and received by Chen Yinglin. The handover was clear on that day. Otherwise, brothers Ma and Chen are still in Guangzhou. How difficult is it to verify? The Northeast has been lost for nearly two decades. Anyone with a conscience is indignant. Therefore, I temporarily followed someone's request and introduced Zhang Juchi to appeal for monthly funding to achieve his great cause. Brother Bonan said that Guangdong's finances are public and he cannot make the decision, and it must be submitted to the Political Affairs Council for approval. Although it was later rejected, even though the gentlemen did not receive the benefit, I still admire Bonan's open attitude. How can it be said that I asked Bonan for activity funds? I hope you will clarify this and dispel the doubts of the people." From this, it can be seen that there is still much estrangement between Guangdong and Li. Moreover, Li, while in Hong Kong, did not agree to go north despite Huang Shaohong's persuasion but stated that he would return to Guangxi for a trip during the day. (February 14th)

Tibetan Monk's Discussion on Tibetan Affairs

More Detailed than What Dharma Master Neng Hai Said; Also Said That the Dalai Has Changed His Attitude Towards the British

Chongqing Dispatch: According to the monk Manduoshi Guolingman, who recently returned to Chongqing from Tibet, the recent situation in Tibet is even more detailed than what Dharma Master Neng Hai, who previously returned to Sichuan from Tibet, said. I am specially recording it below to inform the citizens who are concerned about the situation in Tibet.

Politics

In recent years, all military and civilian affairs in Tibet have been controlled by the Dalai Lama alone. Initially, the Dalai Lama felt that his own power was weak, so he was extremely pro-British, using British imperialism as his backing to consolidate his own position. Recently, his own power has become strong, and the entire Tibet is in his hands alone. Therefore, he is no longer as flattering to the British as before. He extremely opposes any unfavorable actions by the British towards Tibet. Therefore, the current Dalai Lama is not as pro-British as the Dalai Lama of the past.

Economy

The economy of the entire Tibet has been exhausted due to the repeated impact of wars in recent years on the government and the people. The Sichuan-Kang-Tibet war consumed as much as 3 million rupees of the people's wealth. Last May, when the Tibetan army was defeated, the Dalai Lama purchased more than 500,000 yuan worth of military equipment from Britain. Merchants and civilians are sitting and waiting for death due to excessive taxation. Taking Lhasa (the Tibetan capital) as an example, 50 stores have closed down within a month due to the impact of the economy. To purchase goods outside of Tibet, one must exchange them for rupees in India. In the past, four Tibetan silver dollars could be exchanged for one rupee, but now 30 Tibetan silver dollars can only be exchanged for one rupee. In order to collect cash, the Dalai Lama minted copper coins and issued paper money, forcing the people to use them. Now, the assets of the Tibetan people are only copper and paper.

Military

The Tibetan army now only has infantry, cavalry, and artillery. Most of the infantry is drawn from the people and receives very little training. Among them, there are more than 5,000 people who have been trained by the British, Russian, and Japanese, and they are considered the most elite. They are currently stationed in Longbuling and Ka Garden. The military equipment is bought from India and is what India has discarded. Recently, a batch of new-style rifles, machine guns, and mountain guns were purchased from Britain. The uniforms worn by the Tibetan army are all contracted by the British, and their style and color are exactly the same as those of the British soldiers. The flags used by the army have a lion on them, and the colors are red, yellow, blue, white, and black. There are currently about 100,000 soldiers in the army. The soldiers' ages range from 16 to 60. Officers receive 900 liang of barbarian silver per year, in addition to land granted by the Dalai Lama. If they die in battle, the land is inherited by their descendants. In addition to receiving four liang of silver per month, soldiers are also granted some land by the Dalai Lama.

Society

Due to the cold weather in Tibet, there are very few products, and the people's lives are extremely poor. The main foods are nothing more than barley, wheat, and highland barley. The upper class occasionally eats rice, mostly purchased from India. Even the oil and salt for daily use are all transported from India.

People

The Tibetan people can be divided into three parts. One part supports the Panchen Lama, one part supports the Dalai Lama, and the other part is the Red and Yellow sects. The people who support the Panchen Lama often hope that the Panchen Lama will return to Tibet and get rid of the Dalai Lama's harsh rule, but the Panchen Lama has difficulty returning to Tibet because his power is not as strong. (February 23rd)

Achievements of the Shandong Construction Department's Machinery Factory

Long-Distance Telephone and Bucket Dredger

Jinan Dispatch: The long-distance telephone manufactured by the Shandong Construction Department's Transportation and Water Conservancy Machinery Manufacturing Factory previously had a limited communication distance of only over a hundred li due to the use of excessively thick wire for various wire packages. Last winter, another 100 magneto telephones with four magnetos were manufactured, and the magnetos were replaced with tungsten steel. Various wire packages were replaced with No. 43 coated wire, and other parts were also improved. It is now said that 30 units have been installed and tested in many ways. The power of all the rocking generators, earphones, and electric bells is above 110,000 ohms. In addition to the cost of materials, only labor costs are charged, and each unit is priced at 60 yuan, which is about half the price of imported products. It can be said that the price is low and the quality is good. The factory has sent a letter to Shen, the technician of the Electrical Group of the Construction Department, and Hu, the director of the Long-Distance Telephone Management Office, asking them to come to the site for inspection and also asking them to send letters to the construction agencies and long-distance telephone branch offices in various counties, asking them to purchase them separately. The leakage of Shandong's long-distance telephones can be recovered from now on. In addition, the Jinan dredger manufactured by the factory is scheduled to be launched for dredging in the Shili Gate area of the upper reaches of the Xiaoqing River as early as tomorrow (24th). In addition, there are two mud-carrying boats, each of which can hold five cubic meters of mud. During operation, the mud is dredged by the dredger into the boat, and the boat transports it back and forth. When launching the project, Song Wentian, the director of the Xiaoqing River Engineering Bureau, and Zhong Boren, the director of the Machinery Factory, will all be on site to supervise the work. (23rd)
