Local News

Director-General of the Aviation Association, Wu Tiecheng, Hosted Various Teams Yesterday

Reported on Solicitation Methods to Encourage the Teams to Proceed

Wang Xiaolai, Dai Ji, and Others All Gave Passionate Speeches

The China Aviation Association, at 4:30 p.m. yesterday, the solicitation director-general Wu Tiecheng, hosted a tea party for the various team leaders at the YMCA in Baxianqiao. Over two hundred people attended, including Shi Liangcai, Xu Shiying, Wang Yiting, Wang Xiaolai, Lin Kanghou, Du Yuesheng, Chu Huiseng, Qian Xinzhi, Dai Ji, Yu Hongjun, Wen Hongen, Wu Xingya, Pan Gongzhan, and Wang Yunwu. The meeting adjourned at 5:40 p.m. The details are recorded as follows:

Chairman's Speech

The chairman of the Shanghai Solicitation General Team, Wu Tiecheng, said in his speech, "The aviation-rescue-the-nation movement has become increasingly enthusiastic over the past year. Since the establishment of the Aviation Association and the holding of the Aviation-Rescue-the-Nation Propaganda Week, branches have spread to various cities, and the importance of aviation has also been recognized by the people of the whole country. It has now moved from the propaganda period to the implementation period. The greatest purpose of the aviation movement is to unite the wisdom and financial resources of the 400 million people to build an air force and consolidate national defense. Today, the national crisis is deepening. We are here to repent and give speeches. I don't know how tragic the situation is for the people in the combat zones of the three northeastern provinces and Rehe. We will do our best to engage in the most effective national salvation movement, and justice will not allow us to refuse. As the saying goes, 'When impermanence arrives, all things come to an end.' Since the invention of the air force, humans can encounter danger at any time. Its destructive power is greater than that of the army and navy. The strategy and method are very different from the past. It started with swords and guns and evolved into artillery, and now it has evolved from a plane to a three-dimensional one. In the past, the dangers of war were limited to the front line, but now danger is felt everywhere. Although it seems too late to engage in the aviation movement today, we cannot sit idly by and wait for death, and we have to take action quickly. However, this matter is of great importance and cannot be done by the ability of a few people. Therefore, I ask you to take the position of team leader, and I hope that you and the citizens of the city will push it to the whole country, work together with one heart, and assist the Aviation Association. Then the Aviation Association can assist the government to build a strong air force." Next, Zhu Shaoping, the director of the solicitation department, explained the solicitation methods.

Summary of Speeches

(1) Wang Xiaolai said in his speech, "When the people of the country are in danger, they 'always hope for the protection in the air'. In the past, this was superstition, but now it has been seen in fact. When war breaks out, one cannot but hope for protection in the air. The aviation solicitation is also a touchstone of the patriotism of the people." (2) Garrison Commander Dai Ji said in his speech, "I hope that the people of the country should catch up quickly and not just talk about it so that they can see the success as soon as possible." (3) Xu Baoying said, "Aviation thoughts have existed in our country since ancient times. Sun Tzu said, 'Those who are good at fighting move above the nine heavens, and those who are good at defense hide below the nine earths.' The former refers to airplanes, and the latter refers to submarines. Fortunately, the people of the country do not forget their ancestors." (4) Chu Huiseng said, "Assisting the anti-Japanese army and building aviation should be carried out at the same time. Although the establishment of the air force will take at least eight months or a year, the war will certainly not be over in a year. It is not too late to plan for it now. Japan already has more than 70 airplanes donated by the people, but China does not have one. We should catch up quickly." (4) Xie Wugang said, "The people of the country have always been good at writing empty articles and doing little practice. The greatness of Mr. Sun Yat-sen lies in the word 'do'. Mayor Wu can inherit the Prime Minister's ambition and do things practically, which is really admirable. He also cited the Qing Dynasty's use of the funds for building the navy to build the Summer Palace for Empress Dowager Cixi, which led to the decline of the country's power, which can be called a lesson from the past."

Steps to Proceed

(10,000 Yuan Per Team) Each solicitation team should solicit at least 5,000 members or membership fees of more than 10,000 yuan. If the team leader can handle the solicitation independently, it is best. Otherwise, the team leader must invite several colleagues, fellow professionals, colleagues, or family members, relatives, and friends to be team members. Each person is responsible for soliciting a number of members and membership fees, which is determined by the team leader. In this way, solicitation is extremely easy to popularize and is also easy to succeed. (Report in Stages) Once the team members are selected, the team leader should urge the team members to work hard every day. It is hoped that each team member will solicit at least ten members or membership fees of more than 20 yuan per day. Five days after the solicitation, the results will be reported to the team leader once. The team leader will collect the solicitation results of the team members and report them to the general team leader. However, each time there must be more than 1,600 yuan in membership fees or more than 800 members. The reporting dates are divided into six times: the first time is March 15th, the second time is March 25th, the third time is April 5th, the fourth time is April 15th, the fifth time is April 25th, and the sixth time is April 30th. Before reporting the results each time, the membership fees must be paid to the designated bank for collection and the receipt must be obtained as proof of the report. (Efforts to Achieve Universality) The team leader and team members must work hard at any time and in any place and must report the solicitation results on time and do their best to persuade compatriots to join enthusiastically so that people from all walks of life, whether farmers, businessmen, students, men, women, old or young, can participate and spread it throughout the city and the country.

Method of Solicitation

The chairman then introduced Zhu Shaoping to report the methods for forming a solicitation team. (For families,) when members are recruited, in addition to collecting membership fees and issuing receipts, family members, neighbors, relatives, and friends, regardless of gender, age, or occupation, should all be encouraged to join. If relatives and friends are already members, they should be asked to introduce other relatives and friends to join, and so on, with introductions made through mutual referrals. (For schools,) regarding students, in addition to asking the principal and all faculty and staff to join, all students must also be encouraged to join, and students should introduce their relatives and friends to join, and so on, with introductions made through mutual referrals. If students in schools are economically well-off, the school will be responsible for their membership fees, which will be paid by the students upon joining. If students are economically disadvantaged, the school should be responsible for paying their membership fees on their behalf, in one lump sum. The principal will be responsible for collecting the fees paid on behalf of the students in installments. (For shops,) regarding shops, in addition to asking the owner, manager, and senior staff to join, all employees should be encouraged to join as much as possible. Those who have already joined should be asked to introduce relatives and friends to join, and so on, with introductions made through mutual referrals. As for membership fees, they can be paid in installments depending on each person's economic situation, with the shop director or manager responsible for paying the fees on their behalf, in one lump sum, and then deducting them from the employees' pay in installments. (For factories,) regarding factories, in addition to asking the owner, manager, and all other employees to join, they must also be responsible for introducing all workers to join. Workers who have already joined should be asked to introduce relatives and friends to join, and so on, with introductions made through mutual referrals. As for membership fees, they can be paid in installments depending on each person's economic situation, with the factory owner responsible for paying the fees on their behalf, in one lump sum, and then deducting them from the workers' pay in installments. (For organizations,) regarding social organizations and other institutions, in addition to asking all their employees to join, they should also solicit donations from outside.

Aviation Association Hosts Solicitation Team Leader (Photo by Li Zunyong)

Award Method

Award Method of the Shanghai Solicitation Team of the China Aviation Association: (1) Championship Trophy: The person who raises the most donations or donates the most themselves will receive an award certificate and be listed on a commemorative monument. The association will also specially make and present a championship trophy. (2) For team leaders and team members who solicit the fixed quota or exceed the fixed quota, such as team leaders who solicit 10,000 yuan and team members who solicit 1,000 yuan, they will each receive a medal in addition to being listed on a commemorative monument. (3) Commemorative Monument: (a) Individuals who donate 100 yuan or more will be listed on the commemorative monument. (b) Members who, in addition to joining themselves, introduce 50 or more relatives and friends to join this association will be listed on the commemorative monument. (4) Acknowledgment: All donations, regardless of amount, will be acknowledged in the newspaper to promote benevolence.

Xiong Xiling Discusses the Recent Situation in North China

Urgently Awaiting Assistance from Shanghai Residents

Acting Premier Song Ziwen recently launched the Northeast and Rehe Support Association in Beiping, appointing Zhu Qinglan and Xiong Xiling as standing directors, and actively preparing for the implementation of measures, aiming to provide strong military support. It is learned that Xiong Xiling is in charge of the relief group. He arrived in Shanghai from Beiping the night before last, reporting on the recent situation in North China to all sectors of society in Shanghai. At the same time, he discussed with various organizations how to assist the Northeast Volunteer Army and the Rehe Anti-Japanese forces with various important issues. Xiong plans to start working within a few days. Yesterday, our reporter paid a special visit to Xiong at his residence to inquire about the various situations in North China. He provided detailed information. The sections of the conversation that can be disclosed are recorded below.

Rehe Urgently Needs Assistance

Xiong said, "Rehe is the shield of North China. Therefore, since the Japanese army prepared to invade Rehe, our North China military authorities have also urgently planned to resist. Tang Yulin is in charge of Rehe, and the military and volunteer forces in various parts of Rehe are strong and determined to fight the enemy to the death. However, the rear transportation and supply are more difficult due to the terrain of Rehe. Now that the front line is fiercely resisting, rear assistance is particularly important. Therefore, the Northeast and Rehe Support Association is now actively planning to carry out assistance with the most convenient and efficient specific methods. Although Beiping and Tianjin both have local associations, it seems that both associations have local characteristics and cannot plan as a whole. Therefore, in the name of the Northeast and Rehe Support Association, we plan to discuss in detail with all sectors of Shanghai. The most needed items are funds, food, and heavy-duty vehicles. We hope that all sectors of Shanghai will do their best to help."

Tight Defense in Beiping and Tianjin

As for Beiping and Tianjin, our military authorities have been deploying tight defenses since the war broke out in Yuguan. There are considerable forces stationed near Beiping and Tianjin, on high alert.

Speculation on Japanese Military Action

Xiong also said that the Japanese army is determined to occupy Rehe. Therefore, before the outbreak of war in Rehe, they mobilized elite troops and prepared for a long time before launching an invasion. If Rehe is occupied, they will not invade Beiping and Tianjin for the time being. Otherwise, not only Beiping and Tianjin, but also the entire coastline of China will be disturbed by them.

The Central Mint Will Begin Minting on the First of Next Month

The Opening Ceremony Will Be Held That Afternoon

The Central Mint has not officially started minting since its establishment. Recently, the government decided to abolish the tael and change to the yuan to unify the currency system, and the Ministry of Finance ordered that minting officially begin on March 1 to meet the needs. The opening ceremony will be held from 2:00 p.m. to 5:00 p.m. that afternoon, and guests from all sectors of society at home and abroad are invited to visit. Minister of Finance Song Ziwen will also attend the ceremony. All preparations before the start of minting have been completed, and it is reported that the machine test results were very good. After the start of minting, the daily working hours will be tentatively set at ten hours, and it is estimated that 250,000 to 300,000 yuan of new coins will be produced daily. Most of the minting raw materials will be supplied by the Central Bank. In the future, outsiders can also entrust the mint to mint silver on their behalf by paying the prescribed handling fee.

Wu Chaochu Pays Attention to the Protection of Civil Rights in the Constitution

Sends a Letter to Sun Ke Suggesting

Special Provisions Should Be Added

Central Committee Member Wu Chaochu fraudulently sent a letter to President Sun Ke of the Legislative Yuan, saying, "Zhesheng, my dear brother, I have received your letter the other day, in which you have invited me to be a consultant to the Constitution Drafting Committee of the Legislative Yuan. In the future, if you have any questions, I will contribute what I know at any time to help you. Now, I would like to tell you about one thing that I have already thought about. The greatest purpose of the constitution is to seek happiness for the people, and the most important thing to seek happiness for the people is to protect the people's freedom and rights, and the most important thing to protect the people's freedom and rights is to protect the people's personal freedom. In our country, warlords are tyrannical and officials are willful. They arbitrarily trample on the people's personal freedom and often detain them without reason. Detention is not done through legal procedures, and after detention, there is no definite date for interrogation, and they are not released. This leads to long imprisonment and no way to appeal. Even if relatives and friends try to rescue them, there is no way to seek help except through requests and bribes. As a result, some are released without announcing the reason, while others are detained without release, and some are even subjected to private torture. Such dark situations only exist in the so-called chaotic times in our country's history and in Europe in the Middle Ages. Under such circumstances, even if the constitution clearly stipulates the protection of civil rights, it is only equal to a dead letter. Recently, scholars who are concerned about the times have organized societies to protect civil rights in order to remedy the situation, but I am afraid that it will be difficult to achieve significant results. In my opinion, it is impossible to achieve success without clearly stipulating a legal procedure for effective relief. The most comprehensive protection of the people's personal freedom in various countries is in the countries of the Anglo-American legal system. The reason why they can achieve this is due to the provision of the Writ

of Habeas Corpus in the law. When a person is detained by an agency, organization, or individual, he may request the senior court to issue this writ, ordering the detaining party to submit the body of the detained person to the court and state the reason for the detention to the court. The court then examines whether the reason for the detention is legal, but does not try the content of the case. Depending on whether the reason for the detention is sufficient, the court may order release, bail, or remand. This is a good and effective method that is best to emulate. Since the Republic of China, the provisional laws and constitutions promulgated have never failed to clearly state the protection of the people's personal freedom, but in reality, the people's personal freedom has not been protected at all. This is all because the protection is just empty talk, without legal procedures. Therefore, Western philosophers have said that procedural law is more important than substantive law. If the procedures for protection and relief are not prepared, empty talk about principles will not be able to be implemented. I believe that this relief method should be clearly stipulated in the constitution so that civil rights can be effectively protected and the law can be implemented. I respectfully submit my humble opinion to the constitution drafting officials for consideration. I wish you all the best."

Huafeng Company Hosted Guests to Promote Kaicheng's Domestic Sulfuric Acid

Huafeng Company, specializing in industrial raw materials for domestic factories, has been in operation for many years. To promote the domestically produced sulfuric acid of the managed Kaicheng Company, they hosted a banquet for guests from all sectors at the Bankers' Association yesterday afternoon, including Lin Kanghou, Chairman of the National Chamber of Commerce; Wang Xiaolai, Chairman of the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce; Zhu Wenqi, representative of the mercerized cotton weaving industry; Gu Lijiang, representative of the enamel industry; Fang Anpu, representative of the soda industry; and more than forty others, including Zhao Jinqing, Feng Shaoshan, Cui Fuzhuang, Pu Shuhong, Xu Xinliu, and Lu Wenshao. First, the host, Xie Xiaochu, gave a report, stating that sulfuric acid is a widely used raw material, essential for textile factories, dyeing and finishing factories, enamel factories, soda factories, and factories of all sizes. Before Kaicheng Company's invention, the sulfuric acid used by factories mostly depended on Japan and Germany. Although Xiangmao Foreign Firm had products, the prices were too high, the cost too expensive, and millions of dollars were drained away annually. Kaicheng Company spent much effort and many years researching the manufacturing method of sulfuric acid raw materials before succeeding, a significant industry beneficial to society. All of you are leaders in the industry and elders in the business community, and you are always enthusiastic about promoting domestic products. We sincerely hope that you will introduce domestic sulfuric acid to various factories. Next, Fang Yexian, manager of Kaicheng Company, reported on the establishment and products of Kaicheng Company. Subsequently, Lin Kanghou, Wang Xiaolai, and Zhu Wenqi gave speeches successively, expressing their admiration for Huafeng Company's enthusiasm for promoting domestic products, and hoping that they would supply various factories with the lowest possible prices and the best quality goods.

It was decided to make 1,000 cotton vests and 1,000 food bags for the soldiers within ten days as quickly as possible and send them. Then more needed items will be made. However, due to limited financial resources, an advertisement has been published to solicit donations of money and domestic cloth from all sectors, and patriotic ladies are invited to come to the association to help with the work. Furthermore, the clothing for helping refugees that was previously collected has been sent to the Beijing YWCA, and it is still hoped that well-intentioned men and women will continue to send items to the association (Address: 8 Bing, Yuanmingyuan Road, Telephone: 13322).

City Chamber of Commerce Correspondence Class Registration Will Close Soon

The Correspondence Class has been established for several years and has indeed made significant contributions to uneducated merchants. Therefore, with each enrollment, shop employees, both male and female, from this city and other places have rushed to register for admission. The correspondence lectures for this semester focus on commerce. Common sense knowledge such as business methods, bookkeeping methods, transportation insurance, and other teaching materials, and applied writing such as commercial submissions, contracts, and agreements are all tailored to the needs of merchants. The students' practice is especially focused on correction. New student registration closes on March 5th. Tuition is free, and only three yuan is charged for lecture notes every six months.

Ministry of Finance Revises Banking Industry Regulations

The Bankers Association of this city drafted operating regulations last year, which were submitted to the relevant authorities for record in January of this year. The association has now received approval from the Ministry of Finance Qian Zi No. 2007, stating that the submitted regulations and attachments have been reviewed. Except for Article 4, Section 2, and Section 3 of the credit regulations, and the wording of credit transactions and overdrafts, which should all be deleted, a new item should be added after the original text of the same article, stating: "The aforementioned business types should still be handled by each bank in accordance with the articles of association approved by the ministry." And except that the words "such as" in Article 25 are inverted and should be corrected immediately, the rest are without disagreement and should be approved for record. It is heard that the banking industry has already complied with the approval and made changes.

Sending Personnel to Re-Survey the Land Acquisition Case

The case of acquiring civilian land in the Pengpu District for the construction of the new Shanghai North Railway Station, was submitted by the Executive Yuan to the four ministries of Interior, Railways, Finance, and Industry for deliberation. The original plan was maintained. The residents of the district requested reconsideration, arguing that there were thousands of fruit trees on the land, and the residents' losses were too great. The four ministries held another meeting last week, and representatives from the district were also present to explain the situation. It was decided that the Ministry of Railways would re-survey the land. Personnel have now been sent to Shanghai to conduct an on-site inspection. Furthermore, the Ministry of Railways had previously scheduled a meeting in Shanghai on the 25th to explain the special circumstances of establishing the station to all sectors of society, but this has now been postponed.

After the Strike, Merchants and the Husi Union Petitioned

After the rice merchants in this city went on strike, the Hulianyi Association of rice merchants in South Shanghai and various rice merchants jointly formed the Rice Merchant Committee. Yesterday, they also issued a declaration and hosted a press conference. Specifically, at 5:00 PM, they hosted reporters from various newspapers and news agencies at the Taohuagong on Avenue Min-ti-ni in the French Concession to report on everything that had happened, and the long-standing abuses of the Husi using heavy bushels and forcibly collecting bushel fees, the suffering endured by the rice merchants, and the demand for fair bushels. The petition stated: "Petition for a request. It is believed that the cause of this strike dispute is the Husi's heavy bushels, which have been attacked by newspapers in recent days, becoming the target of public criticism. Although the purpose of the strike is said to be to eliminate abuses, it is actually to implement the proposal for fair bushels, creating clever names, which is nothing more than sensationalizing and reversing cause and effect for eliminating abuses, without a thorough solution. If it is implemented according to its proposal, I am afraid that it will only be peaceful for a while, and it will be difficult to seek long-term stability. The Husi deeply fears that the past suffering will be repeated in the future. In order to maintain our inherent livelihood and seek a permanent solution, after the sixth meeting of the council of this association, it was recorded and should be written and submitted. We earnestly request your ministry and bureau to examine and approve, and consider the suffering of the Husi, which has been restricted for a long time. First, allow the Husi to lift the restrictions according to the established mediation principles, and organize the Shanghai Municipal Management Husi Committee by the union, and also request your bureau to send personnel to supervise the handling of the matter (the method will be submitted separately), so as to avoid any obstruction of the Husi's exercise of fair duties, manipulation from the middle, leading to violations of the light bushels, so that the suffering of the Husi can be relieved, the dispute can be easily settled, the bad habit of strikes can also be used as an excuse, people's food is not worried about scarcity, and society is naturally stable. Long-term resistance depends on it. Moreover, in inland areas such as Wuxi, Zhenting, Hangzhou, Hsia Shih, and other rice-producing areas, the Husi are all autonomous, and there is no precedent for being hired. The trading parties can trust and abide by each other. It is not difficult to investigate and imitate, taking the strengths of others to make up for our weaknesses. Why bother with fair bushels? Who believes that all the accumulated abuses can be eliminated and no more serious malpractices will occur than heavy bushels? If we can truly promote benefits and eliminate abuses, how dare the Husi be different? What we do not approve of is the incomprehensive nature. If we do not eliminate evil completely, we will plant evil causes in the future. The Husi will be the first to bear the brunt, not to mention the impact on people's food and security, which is of great importance. Therefore, we have detailed the advantages and disadvantages and submitted a written request, earnestly requesting your ministry and bureau to examine and approve, allow the Husi to lift the restrictions, and manage themselves by the union, so as to cut off the source of disputes and leave a little bit of livelihood, not to wait for orders. Respectfully submitted."

The Second Branch of the Fourth District Cracked Down on a Large Number of Communists

At 8:30 AM yesterday, the Public Security Bureau of the Second Branch of the Fourth District of Zhabei received a secret report that the Shanghai Shangyu Fellow Association at 127 Hengtong Road had a Communist Party meeting in the west wing room. At the same time, Director Wen of the Municipal Public Security Bureau also sent Inspector Dai to the scene. Together with Director Gong Houzhai and Patrol Officer Dai Yizhong, they led service personnel and police to the address and arrested seven members of the Communist Party, confiscating various reactionary leaflets and books, including a copy of "History of the Russian Revolution," a copy of "International Line," and many reactionary slogans from the Shanghai General Labor Union. At about 11:00 AM, another eleven people were arrested. Director Gong interrogated them one by one and sent them to the Public Security Bureau for investigation. After 5:00 PM in the afternoon, Wang Haishan was arrested again. Yesterday Afternoon, a Shooting Incident Caused by the Vietnamese Police in Xinqiao Street

Vietnamese Police Arrested Because Two Women Shared a Rickshaw

The Rickshaw License on the Vehicle Was Torn Off

Bystanders Mediated, Feeling Greatly Indignant

The Vietnamese Police Opened Fire, Killing One Person

| The Vietnamese Police Have Been Placed Under Custody |

Yesterday afternoon at two o'clock, two women were riding in the same rickshaw, traveling north on Minguo Road into Xinqiao Street. When passing the Ningbo Hotel, they were stopped by Annamese police officer No. 427, who claimed that two people could not ride in one rickshaw. At the same time, he tore off the rickshaw's license. The women got out of the car themselves. Because the license was torn off, the rickshaw puller wanted the Annamese police to return it, but the police resolutely refused. He also demanded that the rickshaw puller and the two women be taken to the police station together. The two women claimed they had urgent business and offered to pay a fine of five jiao to settle the matter, but the police officer still refused and blocked and beat the rickshaw puller. This aroused the indignation of bystanders, who gathered to reason and mediate with the police officer. The police officer threatened the crowd with a rifle. Suddenly, there was a loud bang, and a bullet flew out. The crowd scattered in all directions. When the Annamese police officer fired the gun, Zhu Guting, a shop assistant at Renhe Grain Store, No. 61 Shoulu Lane, Xinqiao Street, was the first to be hit. The bullet pierced through his lower abdomen, and fresh blood gushed out. His large intestine also flowed out of his abdomen with the blood, and he died instantly. Behind him, a passerby named Liu Fugao (39 years old), a native of Zhejiang, was also shot in the abdomen. He is now in critical condition at Renji Hospital. After the incident, the French authorities paid close attention to the matter. They believed that it was inappropriate for the Vietnamese police officer to carry firearms while on duty and carelessly injure people, resulting in death. The police officer was ordered to be placed under custody, and the police chief, Mr. Fei Bai, immediately ordered the police officer's immediate superior to conduct a detailed investigation and punish him according to the law, to emphasize the importance of human life.

In another report, Xu Lianzhen and Zhang Fengying, two women from Suzhou, both around 20 years old, lived together at No. 10, Yu Kang Lane, Pi Shaonai Road, outside Xiaobeimen in the French Concession. At 1:30 p.m. yesterday, the two women went out together and wanted to go to the Sincere Company in Beishi. At the entrance of the lane, they hired a rickshaw pulled by a Jiangbei man named Shen Fangrong (who lived on a small boat by the Hebangbian River on Xujiahui Road in the French Concession), which had a three-sided license (i.e., valid in the British, French, and Chinese areas). The two women sat together and traveled east on Minguo Road. When passing the iron gate at the intersection of Dongxinqiao Street and Minguo Road, it was exactly 1:45 p.m. An armed Vietnamese police officer No. 427 from the Mailan Police Station, who was on duty from 12:00 to 4:00, happened to see two women sitting together in the rickshaw, which violated the regulations. The police officer stepped forward to stop them and moved forward to pry off the license nailed to the back of the rickshaw. At that time, the rickshaw puller stopped the rickshaw. The two women in the rickshaw scolded the rickshaw puller for not taking Zilaihuo Street but coming this way. Unexpectedly, it was seen by passersby, who stopped to watch. For a moment, the sound of people arguing became louder and louder, and the number of people gathered increased, and the voices became more and more chaotic. The Vietnamese police officer did not understand Chinese and mistakenly thought that the passersby wanted to make things difficult for him. He wanted to scare away the onlookers with the rifle he was carrying on his shoulder. Unexpectedly, the bullet was loaded and the safety was not closed, causing the trigger to be pulled. The bullet flew out, killing one person and injuring three bystanders. One was Zhu Guting, a 20-year-old Chaozhou man who was the accountant at the Renhe Sugar Food Store opened by Chen Fengyou, a Chaozhou man at No. 134 Dongxinqiao Street. The bullet entered from behind his left shoulder blade and pierced through his chest below his left breast, and he fell to the ground and died instantly. One of the injured was Liu Fugao (a Ningbo man, a friend of a shop assistant at Yuantaiheng Sugar Store on Yangxing Street), who was shot in the abdomen and whose intestines also flowed out. Another was Zhao Changxing (age and origin unknown, living at No. 24, Dawang Temple), who was shot in the left arm. Another was Xu Linsheng (34 years old, a local resident, address unknown), who was shot in the left arm. Because of the extreme pain, they all fell to the ground. At that time, other police officers nearby heard the gunshot and rushed to the scene. They arrested the woman Xu Lianzhen and the rickshaw puller. Zhang fled from the crowd after the incident. Xu and the rickshaw puller, along with the Vietnamese police officer, were taken to the police station for investigation. At the same time, the police station sent an ambulance to take Zhu's body to the Tongren Fuyuan branch mortuary for an autopsy and reported to the court to send someone to examine the body. Liu Fugao, who was injured, was sent to Renji Hospital, and Zhao Changxing was sent to Guangci Hospital for treatment. Xu Linsheng went to a hospital in Jiumudi for treatment. Afterwards, the deputy chief of the French police station, Pu Nanxuan, and the chief detective went to the scene of the incident to investigate the situation and examine Zhu's body. According to hospital news at 1:00 this morning, Liu Fugao had died of his injuries.

Snow Fell in This City Last Night

Lasted About One Hour

In recent days, the weather has been warm and humid. The day before yesterday (the 23rd), it rained all day, and the next morning it cleared up suddenly, but the temperature dropped sharply, and a north wind rose suddenly. Even wearing light fur, one still felt shivering. The wind was still strong yesterday, and the temperature was the same as the day before. At 9:20 p.m., it suddenly snowed, and it stopped after about an hour.

A Young Man, Concerned About National Affairs, Resolved to Join the Army

A Letter to His Father Said

If the Country Exists, the Home Naturally Exists; If the Country is Destroyed, Where is the Home?

Yu Yinwei (22 years old), a native of Huzhou, used to work at the General Post Office on North Sichuan Road. On the 18th of this month, Yu Jun was scheduled to go to the office, but he never returned. Seven or eight days have passed, and he has neither returned home nor gone to the office. His family was very anxious when they suddenly received a letter from Yu Jun from the front line. Only then did they learn that he had disregarded his own safety and joined the volunteer army to go north to fight the enemy. As he was the only son of his parents, the family grieved and cried after receiving the letter. They asked the postmaster of the General Post Office for instructions. The postmaster, sympathetic to Yinwei's ambition to serve the country, agreed to continue to hold his position. If Tu Jun could return to Shanghai soon, he could still work at the post office, so as to relieve his family's worries. The original letter is as follows:

Respectfully to my uncle,

I have not been able to serve you for several days, and I am very worried. But there is really no other way. It is only because the Japanese invaders are strong, occupying the three northeastern provinces, killing our compatriots, and bombing our houses. All kinds of atrocities are unheard of. Thinking about it makes my heart ache. Recently, the newspapers reported that they have invaded Rehe. If this continues, what will be the outcome? That is why I have joined the volunteer army and gone north. Please don't worry. You must know that if the country exists, the home will naturally exist; if the country is destroyed, where will the home be? Now, my friend, Jun, is a graduate of the Municipal North High School and is very fluent in Chinese and Western languages. Now that he is idle at home, I beg my uncle to find a place for him. Please, please. When I defeat the Japanese army and flatten Fusang, I will see you again. The military bugle is sounding again, so I will end this hastily. (Below omitted)

Tragedy of a Night Shift Liner Crashing into an Oil Tanker

Two Crew Members Drowned in Their Sleep The Entire Cargo of Kerosene Floated on the River Surface

Ma Changyuan, a Shaoxing halogen basket boat, loaded 550 barrels of kerosene from the Shanghai Qiaji Kerosene Company, intending to go to Shaoxing for unloading. He arrived at Song at noon the day before yesterday and docked at the Baotaiwan Customs, opposite the Dongpu beach where the ship was stationed. Because of the formalities such as customs declaration and signing, he could not leave the port that day and waited until dawn to set sail. Unexpectedly, before dawn (at 4:00 a.m. on the 24th), a Yangtze River liner leaving Shanghai passed near the place where the sailboat was docked and broke the bow of Ma Changyuan's ship, which sank immediately. As a result, the crew members Zhao Ajiu, 40 years old, and Zhou Erba, 33 years old, both from Shaoxing, who were sleeping in the bow cabin, could not escape and fell into the water with the ship. They have disappeared and are believed to have drowned. The captain, Wang Erlong, and six other crew members were awakened from their sleep and, seeing that they were in danger, cried out for help. They were rescued by nearby boatmen. All the kerosene on board was lost and floated on the river surface, resulting in huge losses. After causing the accident, the ship not only did not stop to rescue but also sped away. After being rescued and reborn, Captain Wang Erlong immediately reported to the Zhanghuabang River Affairs Office. The deputy river affairs officer took a boat to the scene of the accident for a week of investigation before returning to the office. He then reported the situation to the river affairs office to investigate the name of the ship that caused the accident in order to clarify the truth and facilitate negotiations.

The Chicago Exposition Seeks Famous Paintings by Fang Junbi

Eight Recent Works Have Been Sent

The Chinese Collection Exhibition of the Chicago Exposition in the United States has recently opened in Shanghai and will soon be shipped to the United States for display. He Bingxian, the person in charge of the exhibition, believes that Oriental art is famous in the world, but there are too many oil paintings this time, which is not enough to promote national glory. Therefore, he discussed with Ms. Fang Biju (wife of Tieci Zeng Zhongwu), a famous painter, and obtained her consent to collect her latest masterpieces: [Riding a Donkey in Fine Rain Through Jianmen], [Fishing Alone in the Cold River Snow], [A Child's Sleep], [Chrysanthemum], [Plum Blossom], [Taoist Priest], [Lushan Waterfall], [Still Life]. These eight paintings will add luster to the entire exhibition. Ms. Fang graduated from the French Higher School of Fine Arts and was a disciple of the famous French painters Inbert and Bernard. Her works have been selected for the Paris Art Exhibition several times. Various newspapers have commented that her works have a delicate and profound thought and are free from any artificiality. She can integrate the strengths of the East, West, South, and North and is regarded as an outstanding female painter in the East. After returning to China, National Guangdong University and Zhixin School successively hired her as a professor.

Zhengtai Rubber Factory Provides Compensation to the Families of Workers Who Died Tragically

The details of the case of the Zhengtai Rubber Factory No. 1 on Tangshan Road in this city, where more than 80 male and female workers were burned to death in an electrical fire a few days ago, have been recorded in previous issues of this newspaper. It is now known that the shareholders of the factory, in consideration of the fact that the deceased workers suffered a tragic death, which is truly pitiful, have specially given each bereaved family a compensation fee of 300 yuan, and the families have issued receipts to collect the money. It is said that two-thirds of the families have already received the money, and the factory is now notifying the families who have not received the money to go and collect it. As for the workers who were not affected, in addition to the regular monthly salary for one month, those who return home for recuperation will be given some travel expenses. After the repair of the factory building of Factory No. 1 is completed, they will be notified to return to work. In addition, it is reported that the bodies of 81 male and female workers who died in the factory have been placed in silk cotton quilts by Pushan Villa and are temporarily stored in the Xinjiangyin Public Office. After the completion of the factory's own cemetery in the Dachang Township area, they will be moved there for burial. The cemetery covers an area of more than three mu and is surrounded by high walls, which is very spectacular. Special personnel will be sent to pay tribute during the spring and autumn seasons to comfort the spirits.

The Ford Motor Company in the United States Resumes Normal Operations

Suspended for Several Days in January Due to External Influences

The car bodies used for passenger vehicles by the Ford Motor Company in the United States are mostly supplied by the Brigg Body Company. In January of this year, some workers at the Brigg factory went on strike. As a result, Ford's source of passenger car bodies was greatly reduced, and this agency did not belong to Ford and could not be controlled. Therefore, it had to be temporarily suspended. For a time, the rumor that Ford factories in various places were on strike was due to this. Fortunately, after a few days, the labor unrest at the Brigg factory subsided, and the supply of passenger car bodies was restored as before. The Ford factories also resumed normal operations. In fact, the Ford Motor Company in the United States has always treated its workers very well, which is well known in the world. There has never been any so-called labor unrest.

The Appeal of Two Kidnappers Was Rejected

The Original Sentence of 20 Years Imprisonment Was Upheld

Lu Heshang and Yu Haitao, two kidnappers from Tongzhou, kidnapped Hengfu, the eight-year-old grandson of Zhang Yunji, a Ningbo businessman who lived at No. 59 Ga'en Road in the French Concession, at 4:20 p.m. on November 24th of last year, with the help of their accomplices. The kidnappers escaped in a cargo truck, and the family of the victim hired a rickshaw puller, Mao Xiaotao, to chase them from behind and shout for help. The detectives intercepted the kidnappers at the intersection of Fuli Road and Jufu Road, rescued the victim, and sent Lu and Yu to the Second Special District Court. They were sentenced to 20 years of imprisonment each. Because Lu and Yu felt that the sentence was too heavy, they expressed their dissatisfaction with the original judgment and filed an appeal with the Third Branch of the Higher Court. The court has already opened a trial and concluded the case, waiting for sentencing. The details have been recorded in previous newspapers. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Zhou, accompanied by assessors Guo and Fan, and Chief Prosecutor Zhao Shibei, came to the Third Criminal Court at 3:00 to bring in the appellants to pronounce the judgment. The appeal was rejected. They also explained the reasons for the judgment to the appellants, saying that kidnapping cases should be punishable by death. The original sentence of 20 years imprisonment was already a lenient reduction. Your appeals are unreasonable, so the judgment is rejected. After the pronouncement, the appellants were returned to custody to await instructions.

Cai Shutang, Manager of Biefa Pharmacy, Was Accused of Embezzlement

Ren Chunrong, a native of Shaoxing, opened the Biefa Pharmacy at No. 819 on the corner of Zha Road and Kader Road in August of last year with his own funds, with a capital of more than 40,000 yuan. He hired Cai Shutang, a native of Ningbo, as the manager. After opening for several months, the business was not prosperous, so he announced the liquidation at the end of January of this year. All the account books of the pharmacy were entrusted to accountant Xie Chunpu for liquidation. During the liquidation, accountant Xie discovered that manager Cai Shutang had embezzled a huge sum of 6,792.22 yuan. He reported this to Ren Chunrong, who reported it to the Jing'an Temple Police Station the day before yesterday. The Chinese detective Wang Yongjun was sent to No. 11 Yian Lane, Kader Road, to arrest Cai and take him to the police station for detention. Yesterday morning, he was sent to the Eighth Criminal Court of the First Special District Court. The plaintiff, Ren Chunrong, hired lawyers Xie Chunming and Zhang Qingtong to appear in court. Lawyer Wang of the police station stated the case, saying that an important witness in the case, Xu Fushou, the accountant of the pharmacy, had returned to his hometown of Shaoxing and was unable to appear in court today. He requested a postponement. Ren Chunrong also complained that accountant Xie had discovered that the defendant had embezzled the above-mentioned amount, but there were still accounts that could not be clarified for a while. When questioned, the defendant Cai Shutang confessed that since the preparation and opening of Biefa Pharmacy, he had been hired by Ren as the manager, and the accountant Xu Fushou was hired by Ren. The pharmacy's capital was said to be more than 40,000 yuan, but more than 20,000 yuan of it was taken away by Ren for other transactions. The remaining amount was clearly accounted for and signed by him, including more than 4,000 yuan for the purchase of business property and decoration, 1,600 taels for the small house rental, 100 taels per month for rent, 6,000 yuan for medicine dispensing fees, and more than 2,000 yuan for printed materials and bottle materials, all of which can be verified by clear accounts. Therefore, not only did he not embezzle, but there was still a surplus of funds in the pharmacy, because Ren owed him more than 1,000 yuan for room rent and miscellaneous expenses, as the pharmacy's pharmaceutical factory rented his remaining house, with a monthly rent of 70 yuan, which had not been paid for eight months, etc. Finally, the defendant's lawyer requested that the defendant be allowed to be released on bail during the adjournment. Judge Wu Tingqi verified the confession and ordered Cai to be released on bail of 3,000 yuan from a shop. The case was adjourned for further hearing.

The Hearing of the Case of the Gauze Exchange Was Concluded

During the Japanese invasion of Shanghai on February 9th of last year, the Gauze Exchange closed all transactions of its clients, and the clients, including Sha Weiyi, filed a lawsuit for confirmation. The Exchange lost in the first instance and filed an appeal, adding lawyers Liu Chongyou and Zhang Shizhao. The case was repeatedly tried by Mr. Hu Yigu, the former presiding judge of the Civil Division of the Second Higher Court, and the debate had been concluded. Unexpectedly, before the sentencing date, the case was changed to a re-opening of the debate. After Judge Hu resigned, Judge Li Lian continued to hold several hearings and investigated in detail. Yesterday afternoon at 2:00, the last hearing for the conclusion of the debate was held. The appellant lawyers from both sides were present, and Wu Mo, a lawyer, was added to the side of Sha Weiyi to appear in court. The debate between the two sides was very intense. When the court adjourned, it was already dusk. Judge Wu announced that the case would be sentenced on March 4th at 1:00 p.m.

The Case Against the Star Daily Was Concluded

Chen Dieyi Fined 50 Yuan

The Star Daily was accused by the police station of publishing advertisements for Huang Shifeng's medical treatment and Detang Hospital's amenorrhea and menorrhagia medicines on February 9th, which the police station's security department considered to be related to morality. The editor-in-chief of the newspaper, Chen Dieyi, was summoned to the First Special Court on the morning of the 18th for a trial. Huang Shifeng and Shang Daosheng, the manager of Detang Hospital, were summoned to testify, and the trial was adjourned for one week. The trial was continued in the Second Court yesterday morning. First, lawyer Li Zhishan of the police station stated the case, accusing Chen Dieyi of publicly introducing abortion methods in violation of Article 308 of the Criminal Code, Article 44 of assisting the principal offender, and Article 251 of the Publication Law of disseminating or selling obscene texts and pictures. The witness Huang Shifeng did not arrive, and only Shang Daosheng appeared in court, admitting that he had published the advertisement. Next, Chen Dieyi was questioned. Chen confessed that the police station had not taken any action against the medical and pharmaceutical parties who published advertisements in the Star Daily, and the Star Daily had no right to refuse to publish their advertisements. Moreover, publishing advertisements was different from publishing news. If there was any meaning of recommending others in the news, he should be responsible. As for the advantages and disadvantages of medical advertisements, he had not tried them and could not distinguish them, so he could not take the blame for others. Then, Shao Shengzu, the lawyer representing the defendant, stood up to defend, saying that advertising was a business nature. The advertisement belonged to a formal doctor and hospital, and the medicine had been sold for many years. The police station had not investigated and banned it, and there were no words of war or public introduction of abortion methods in the advertisement, so the crime of Article 308 could not be established. As for the article of Article 251, which disseminates or sells obscene texts and pictures, only the names of medicines are found in the advertisement, and there is no obscenity at all, so this crime cannot be established. The clause in Article 14 is [assisting the principal offender is an accomplice]. Now, since there is no principal offender, it is even more ridiculous to add the name of an accomplice to our client. In short, the police station does not ban or sue the abortion of idlers that the police station considers, but accuses our client of having a criminal act, which is a complete abandonment of the root and pursuit of the branch, and should be ordered to be innocent. At this point, Judge Wu declared the debate concluded and sentenced Chen Dieyi to a fine of 50 yuan for the crime of introducing abortion by writing. Chen Dieyi stated in court that he would give up the appeal and then tried other cases.

Negotiation Between Mei Lanfang to Film Farewell My Concubine

The Contract Fee Must Be 100,000 Yuan; If Filmed, It Will Not Be Performed Again

After the famous actor Mei Lanfang was hired by the Tianchan Stage at a high price to come to Shanghai to perform, he did not return north after the expiration of his contract and temporarily resided in Shanghai. Recent News of the Severe Disaster in the Northwest

Demolishing Houses, Selling Materials, Selling Daughters, and Selling Sons

Digging Graves and Opening Coffins in Hopes of a Single Meal

The Jiangsu Disaster Prevention Association on Sixth Avenue in this city received a telegram yesterday from Yang Shuzhi, a representative of the Xiaohui Yizhen Association of Beiping, who went to Shaanxi to investigate the disaster. The telegram stated that Shaanxi has suffered from continuous drought for five years, and the disaster is severe and unprecedented. To this day, the suffering is even more intense. The people of the country are currently struggling with national difficulties and seem to no longer pay attention to these starving compatriots. As a result, those in Shaanxi who are trying to provide relief are shouting and pleading, but with little effect. Yang Shuzhi was entrusted by his association to come to Shaanxi to investigate the disaster. As soon as he arrived in the Tanshibao area of Xi'an, he saw piles of building materials from houses that had been demolished and sold by the disaster victims, stacked like mountains. Tools and belongings were scattered on the ground, and the selling victims were all gaunt and skeletal, with glowing eyes like ghosts. Their eyes were filled with tears, and they wanted to cry out. As soon as a passerby stopped, they would grab at their clothes and beg them to buy something. When asked about their hometowns, most of them were from Fufeng, Wu Gong, Qishan, Mei County, Qian County, and Liquan, with some from Jingyang, Xianyang, Xingping, and Yuan County. Gray-haired old women led their daughters to sell, and young men knelt and called out "Father" to potential buyers, filling the streets, a scene too unbearable to watch. Even more tragic, tombs in the Jingyang area were being dug up, and every temple was being demolished. It is said that the timber from the demolished temples could be sold, and clothes could be obtained from the excavated tombs. Moreover, most of the people digging up the graves were their own children, who were either unwilling to dig but could not avoid it. They exposed the bones of their ancestors and sold the coffins of their deceased to obtain a single meal. Nothing could be more cruel than this. Now, even searching for grass seeds to fill their stomachs or digging up turnips for food is no longer possible. Furthermore, the new wheat seeds were sown after the snow and have not been properly watered, and many have withered and died. If it does not rain again in ten days, the harvest will be hopeless. This kind of situation is heartbreaking to see. Relief can be divided into two types: work relief and emergency relief. The disaster in Shaanxi was caused by, in addition to the opium poppy cultivation, inconvenient transportation, undeveloped water conservancy, and stagnant industry. If we can enthusiastically donate funds and work with Shaanxi to build more car routes to facilitate transportation, complete the Jing River and Wei River diversion projects, dig more self-flowing wells to develop water conservancy, and establish spinning and weaving factories to revitalize industry, then the current disaster victims can avoid death by working, and future disasters can also be prevented. This is the best of the work relief measures. For the widowed, orphaned, old, and weak, who are on the verge of death and cannot benefit from work relief, nothing is better than establishing porridge kitchens and distributing dry food. This is the most urgent form of emergency relief. I implore you to generously assist and do your best to promote it.

New Resolution on the French Municipal Council's Cross-Boundary Road Construction and Telephone

Submitted to the Shanghai Municipal Council of the International Settlement

The Shanghai Times reported that the French Municipal Council submitted a resolution to the Shanghai Municipal Council of the International Settlement yesterday regarding the cross-boundary road construction and telephone contract. The content was not disclosed by either party. However, the Shanghai Times reporter learned from reliable sources that the French authorities no longer have any problems with the Shanghai Telephone Company including the extra rental fee for each telephone stipulated in the contract in the company's arrears account and considering it again when adjusting the telephone fee in 1931. However, they believe that the money reported to the Chinese authorities should be borne by the company or the users of the International Settlement, and should not be included in the arrears account, so that all users jointly and indirectly bear the burden, because the cross-boundary road areas are adjacent to the International Settlement and have nothing to do with the French Concession. According to the company's estimate, the extra rental fee will only indirectly cost each user a few cents per quarter. This resolution of the French Municipal Council will cause this long-standing issue to be disputed again.

Reorganization of Newspaper Sales on the Beijing-Shanghai Railway

Directly Distributed by the Newspaper Association

All Newspapers Sold at the Listed Price

Newspaper sales on the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo railway lines have always been contracted by merchants through bidding by the railway bureau. Occasionally, merchants focus on profit and neglect service. Newspaper prices are not fixed, and private sales are unavoidable. Furthermore, the trains also sell sundries and merchandise, which is noisy and annoying to passengers. Therefore, the railway bureau canceled the sale of sundries last year and only sold books and newspapers. At the end of January this year, when the contract with the contractor for the Beijing-Shanghai line expired, the railway bureau signed a method for distributing books and newspapers on trains with the Shanghai Newspaper Association, while simultaneously canceling merchandise and reducing the bid price (the previous bid was 550 yuan per month, now reduced to 500 yuan). All book and newspaper sales on the trains will be directly distributed by the Shanghai Newspaper Association and sold at the listed price on each newspaper. The association has a price list for compliance, without any private increases. Magazines, pictorials, and Western newspapers will also be sold to serve passengers. All newspaper sellers will be strictly trained by the association, wearing neat uniforms and badges. Furthermore, the railway bureau believes that there are many passengers at the five major stations of Suzhou, Wuxi, Changzhou, Zhenjiang, and Nanjing, and there should also be newspaper sales facilities.

Reader's Counselor

Working and Falling in Love

[Letter from Wei Yingjun, this city]

Dear Editor: I am currently an apprentice worker in a national goods factory. Due to my poor family, I often dropped out of school during my childhood, but fortunately, I was able to graduate from elementary school. After graduation, I studied in a mainland store, but the life was certainly not satisfactory to me. Last winter, due to various circumstances, I came to Shanghai to seek employment. Unexpectedly, I became an apprentice worker. I work hard during work hours and think hard during my free time. It has been three months since then. Some people have ridiculed me as a worker who is not even as good as a worker, yet I am still at ease. How boring and meaningless is that?

I think this decadent and irrelevant ridicule is unconscious ridicule, and there is absolutely no need to reply. In my hometown, family, friends, and relatives, no one would have thought that I would become a worker. Many even praised me, saying: "With your diligence in reading, the heavens will not fail those who work hard. Now that you have come to Shanghai, you are happy! You are enjoying life!" Whenever I see such words, I hate that I have read so few books and cannot use extremely painful words to express my life and intentions. For myself, I proudly never relied on family or relatives to make a living and was able to be self-reliant through hard work. I felt comforted in my heart. However, whenever I think that working is not a long-term plan, not only will my family be hurt when they hear about it, but if my other friend knows about it, we will both lose our lifelong happiness. Whenever I think of this, my heart aches. This "other friend" is my lifelong partner. Every man at a certain age wants to love; I am no exception. Let me tell you about it! When I was studying in a mainland store, the store owner's daughter considered me based on my daily actions and abilities. Half a year after I entered the store, she fell in love with me. I was very surprised by this romance because her talent, appearance, and advice were all pleasing to me. After half a year of friendship and love, last winter, she came to tell me every night that she had discussed our marriage with her mother, and to her delight, the old lady did not object. However, her father still thought in the old way, "Raising a daughter is hoping for a high-ranking family." If you can find a better job, this marriage will not be difficult to achieve, and you can be sure of it. That's what she told me. Originally, I was not accustomed to the life in the store, and the various actions of the merchants made me dissatisfied. After hearing her words, I immediately told her, "I will definitely change my job." I said changing jobs was very likely because I had already found a trainee position in Shanghai through a friend's recommendation. "Life is not always as you wish, eight or nine times out of ten." Due to illness, I arrived in Shanghai only five days late. When I arrived, the trainee position had already been filled by someone recommended by the factory's shareholders. Therefore, I resolutely became a worker. I was extremely sorry to her. Every time she writes, she expresses her passionate feelings and says that her father has agreed, but we must wait until I am promoted to a staff member before we can officially get engaged, with a deadline of two years. This letter arrived a week ago, and she has urged me to reply twice this week. I hesitated for a long time. Abandoning her, unless I never marry for the rest of my life, otherwise, it will be difficult to find this kind of qualified woman again. There are many good women in the world, but how can they be willing to marry a poor man without talent or wealth? Besides, she has never let me down, and has never despised me for being poor and chaste. She even helped me economically to buy books. How can I bear to abandon this affection? If I agree to her conditions, I know her father's character well. His words and deeds have never changed in the slightest. He has limited me to being promoted to a staff member within two years. With my talent and learning, having only studied for six years, and the overstaffing in Chinese society, I think reaching promotion to a staff member in two years is only a dream! Moreover, I fundamentally hope to study the meaning of industrial work. The facts of the past three months have proven this to me. Although my face is covered in mud and my clothes are stained with oil, I am not discouraged by this. On the contrary, I often tell myself: "If the typical Chinese life can be like this, at least we can hope to be on par with the great powers." As for my personal life, what is the interest in being a staff member or a trainee, except for more money? In short, I feel that being an apprentice, except for being scolded and beaten, and suffering physical losses, my spirit is extremely happy! Sometimes I really want to honestly tell my father and her, but I never have the courage. Now, because of her letter, I am touched by everything. The thinking of older people is: work is humble, work is ignorant and uneducated! Dear Editor: Being in such a complex environment, how should I deal with it? My personal mind and brainpower feel too short to apply. Please, sir, give me some advice. How should I reply to her? How should I deal with my family? Reply will be published tomorrow. Sun Shenfang's lofty friendship is commendable.

After this column revealed Mr. Wu of Zhenhai's letter "Nowhere to Go" (see this column on the 21st of this month), we immediately received a letter from Mr. Sun Shenfang of this city, willing to use his personal strength to help Mr. Wu continue his studies. His enthusiasm is truly admirable. In addition to forwarding the letter to Mr. Wu and asking him to contact Mr. Sun directly, this column believes that Mr. Sun's enthusiasm is rare and should not be ignored. Therefore, we will commend him in this column and thank Mr. Sun on behalf of Mr. Wu.

In preparation, the association will continue to assign uniformed newspaper sellers to sell various Shanghai newspapers at the five stations. The prices will be the same as those sold on the trains. This is the spirit of pure service of the Newspaper Association. The Beijing-Shanghai Railway Bureau strives to facilitate passengers, so they cooperate with each other. One reduces the bid amount, and the other sells at the listed price. From then on, the order of the railway will be well-organized, noise can be avoided, and newspaper prices will be uniform, without causing confusion. This is what the authorities and passengers hope for. The above-mentioned measures were implemented on March 1st. From now on, if passengers encounter newspaper sellers with price differences or lack of courtesy, they can point out their badge number, date, and train number at any time and send a letter to the Shanghai Newspaper Association for investigation and improvement.

Russian Commits Suicide Due to Melancholy

[Hangs Himself on his Name Day Due to Sentimental Reflections]

Russian Chetinov, 36 years old, worked as a chauffeur at the Asia Petroleum Company and lived in the company's warehouse at 2843 Yangshupu Road. The day before yesterday was his name day. It is unknown what stimulated him, but he suddenly had thoughts of ending his life. He went alone to a bathroom in his residence and hanged himself with a silk scarf on a tap pipe. He was discovered later, already dead. The Yangshupu Police Station was immediately notified and sent detectives to investigate. His body was taken to the Philen Road Coroner's Office. Yesterday morning, the First Special District Local Court was requested to send Prosecutor Guo Wei to the office to examine the body and open a public case. According to the Western detective's report, the deceased had been working as a driver at the Asia Company for seven years. He was usually diligent and thrifty, so he still had a passbook with 800 yuan in savings. Therefore, his sudden suicide was not suspected to be due to economic problems. However, he had a wife and daughter, whom he divorced for some reason 14 years ago, so his wife and daughter are now in his hometown. The day before yesterday was his name day, and according to custom, he was supposed to invite guests to celebrate. Presumably, because his wife had separated from him and was not present, he felt depressed and had thoughts of death. Furthermore, according to Russian Qu Tinav, the deceased was his cousin, and he is now claiming the body. After hearing the confession, Mr. Guo ruled that the deceased Russian Chetinov had hanged himself before death. The body was handed over to Qu Tinav with a guarantee to take it back for coffin and burial.

Gan Jianxian Passes Away

Gan Jianxian, brother of Gan Jingxian, lawyer of the Shanghai Municipal Council's legal group, was the beloved son-in-law of Tang Shaoyi, a famous figure in diplomatic circles. He graduated from New York University in the United States and worked in the accounting department of the Beijing-Shanghai Railway Bureau for many years. He was always diligent in his work and was highly valued by his superiors. He fell ill due to overwork and took leave to be treated at the Guangci Hospital. However, Heaven did not grant him many years, and he died in the hospital on the 23rd night at the young age of 42. Relatives and friends were deeply saddened by the news. His brother, lawyer Gan Jingxian, was particularly grieved and asked for leave for a few days to assist with the funeral arrangements. Yesterday, those who went to the Gan residence to offer condolences included Shanghai Mayor Wu Tiecheng, Municipal Government Secretary-General Yu Hongjun, Jianghai Customs Supervisor Tang Haian, and others. The remains have been moved to the Universal Funeral Home on Jiaozhou Road in western Shanghai for coffin and burial. The funeral will be held at 1:30 PM on the 27th. At that time, those who go to express their condolences will definitely be a grand procession of plain cars and white horses.

Mao Quantai Furniture Store General Factory Resumes. Mao Quantai Furniture Store has been in business for more than 30 years and has a good reputation. Not only does it have special influence in the Nanyang Islands and the Guangzhou and Hong Kong areas, but the number of Chinese antique furniture shipped to the United States every year is quite large. It is one of the leading large furniture stores in Shanghai. The issuing office is located on North Sichuan Road, and the general factory is located on Tiyuhui Road. During the January 28th Incident last year, the general factory was hit by artillery fire and suffered heavy losses. After much planning by General Manager Mao Yuxiang, the factory has now been completely restored to its original state. The factory site is larger than before, covering more than 20 acres. The buildings are sturdy and beautiful, and the interior and exterior arrangements are even better than before. There are more than 500 craftsmen. The factory has perfect equipment and adopts scientific management methods. Workers' security is guaranteed, and safety is ensured. Therefore, they all work diligently. There are two large storage rooms that can accommodate more than 300 sets of furniture. The work part is divided into the sawmilling department, the installation department, the carving department, the white body department, the Chinese lacquer department, the foreign paint department, the tailoring department, and the insulation department. The insulation department is particularly unique. Chinese lacquer requires a constant temperature to achieve fine workmanship, and this type of equipment is rare in other furniture stores. As for accessories, such as springs and glass, they are directly ordered from various countries without any borrowing. The various room furniture styles strive for artistic modernization. Specially hired technicians design them, which is praised by all sectors. Introduction of Domestically Produced Electroplating Raw Materials. China has always produced a large quantity of copper and tin utensils. Since the invention of polishing and electroplating, the application of copper utensils has become more widespread. Some are specially polished without electroplating, such as steel signs, copper railings, copper beds, and all kinds of copper, tin, steel, and fine utensils. Others are polished and then nickel-plated, such as flashlights, thermos bottles, and various supplies such as wheels and clocks. As society progresses, the polishing and plating industry becomes more developed. Unfortunately, the raw materials required are all imported, so a huge amount of money is leaked every year. The China North Factory in this city previously produced and sold Shuangjian brand copper polishing oil, which was indeed cheap and of good quality, and was able to sell well throughout the country. The Japanese goods, such as Nissan Brand, etc., which had been on the market have now disappeared. This is also a practical anti-Japanese work. It is heard that the China Factory is not satisfied with this and continues to research diligently. Recently, it has also produced a nickel polishing white oil, the effect of which is the same as the best American goods. A large batch will be shipped next month. Dealers in various ports are very welcome to sign contracts for distribution. The factory's office is located next to the Shen Bao Newspaper Office on Hankou Road.

Ou Jun has extensive experience in the hotel industry and will be praised by all sectors at that time.

Weather Report

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated: The coastal areas of Shandong are cloudy with signs of change. Wind force is unstable. The Yangtze River basin is overcast with rain or fog. Winds are from the northeast to southeast. This is due to a low-pressure area forming in southwestern China. The coastal areas south of Ma'an Island and within the Taiwan Strait are clear with a gentle northeasterly wind. Letter to the Editor

To the Esteemed Editor of Shen Bao,

Regarding the report in your newspaper yesterday about the sale of land by Jing'an Temple to support the military, there is a slight error. The land of our temple absolutely cannot be sold. It is only that the land on the left and right sides of the mountain gate was leased to Samsung Company (not Fulushou Company). This company is also enthusiastic about patriotism, so last month they advanced 5,000 yuan in rent to support the Northeast Volunteer Army. There is no other amount, and Zhiba has no involvement whatsoever. Please correct this quickly to avoid misunderstandings from the outside world. I am deeply grateful.

Respectfully,

Zhiba, Abbot of Jing'an Temple

Jiangsu Province Secondary Schools Launch Campaign for Teachers and Students to Purchase Aircraft

Zhenjiang Normal School advocates for teachers and students to jointly purchase one aircraft. Jiangsu Middle School students advocate for students to independently purchase one aircraft. Jiangsu Provincial Zhenjiang Normal School previously launched a campaign to unite teachers and students of secondary schools throughout the province to donate funds to purchase an aircraft. The fundraising method is as follows: 1. Purpose: To use the strength of teachers and students in provincial, county, and private secondary schools throughout Jiangsu Province to donate funds to purchase one aircraft. 2. Price: Between 100,000 and 150,000 yuan. 3. Implementation steps: (a) The school (Provincial Zhenjiang Normal School) will suggest to the Secondary School Joint Association to request its approval. (b) The school will suggest to the Secondary School Teachers Association to request its approval. (c) Suggest the Education Department instruct various public and private secondary schools to endorse this proposal. 4. Donations: It is hoped that (a) each student will donate at least one yuan; (b) each teacher will donate at least 20% of one month's salary. 5. Savings institution: Entrust the National Bank. 6. Donation custodians: In addition to three representatives each from the Middle School Joint Association and the Middle School Teachers Association, three representatives each will also be nominated by county and private middle schools, and the Director of the Education Department will be the ex-officio guarantor.
