U.S. Government Sends Note to League of Nations

Acknowledges that the Recommendations Are in Accordance with U.S. Intentions

Method and Scope Should Preserve Independent Judgment

Important Declaration is Being Drafted

(Washington) After consultations between Secretary of State Stimson and Hull, a telegram containing an important document on the U.S. position in the Sino-Japanese dispute was sent to the League of Nations, stating that the U.S. government's intentions in this dispute are largely in accordance with those of the League of Nations, and that their common goal is to maintain peace and resolve international disputes peacefully. The U.S. government intends to make every effort to support the League of Nations' efforts, while reserving its independent judgment regarding methods and scope. The League of Nations' factual determinations are consistent with the U.S. government's understanding of the facts based on reports from U.S. representatives. The U.S. government has generally agreed with the League of Nations' conclusions. Regarding the declaration of the non-recognition of "Manchukuo" principle and the expression of its attitude on this issue, the League of Nations and the United States are in a common position. The U.S. government expresses general agreement with the principles of such a recommendation based on the treaties it has signed, and sincerely hopes that China and Japan, which have long had friendly relations with the United States and other countries, can take into account the existing clear expression of world public opinion and make their policies compatible with the wishes and needs of all countries to resolve their disputes peacefully. (25th Reuters Dispatch)

(Washington) It is reported that Secretary of State Stimson and the incoming Secretary of State Hull held a meeting at the State Department today and decided to issue a declaration. The declaration is currently being drafted and will generally express strong support for the League of Nations' condemnation of Japan's Manchurian policy. The meeting between Stimson and Hull was held after receiving a notice from the League of Nations General Assembly stating that the League of Nations had passed a resolution inviting the Soviet Union and the United States to participate in the League of Nations' efforts to mediate the Sino-Japanese dispute. (25th Reuters Dispatch)

The Time Has Matured to Invoke Article 16 Against Japan

Lytton Will Urge Government to Fulfill Treaty Obligations

Japan's Treaty Violations Cannot Be Tolerated

(London) Lord Lytton, speaking in Godalming today, referred to the Sino-Japanese dispute, saying that if the time has matured for the League of Nations to declare the application of the sanctions methods contained in Article 16 of the Covenant, he hoped that Britain would be prepared to fulfill its treaty obligations. He firmly believes that the solution he proposed is the only one that fits the facts. We must make Japan understand that the League of Nations cannot tolerate actions that violate the rules. More importantly, we must make Japan understand our sincerity in seeking a solution within the rules. (24th Reuters Dispatch)

The Anglo-Japanese Alliance Still Lingers in His Mind

Japanese Foreign Ministry Prepares Withdrawal Procedures

Cabinet Decision Will Be Followed by Consultation with Privy Council

Withdrawal Time Approximately in Mid-March

(Tokyo) The Foreign Ministry has begun drafting a concrete plan for consulting the Privy Council regarding withdrawal from the League of Nations, divided into four parts: (1) The notice to be submitted to the League of Nations Secretariat regarding the withdrawal; (2) The matter of revising the Treaty of Versailles due to the submission of the notice; (3) The obligations to be borne by the Japanese government for two years after submitting the notice; (4) The handling of the Disarmament Conference, the Labor Conference, and other international conferences hosted by the League of Nations. The above four documents will take several days to complete. Therefore, the Cabinet will decide on this consultation proposal and submit it to the Privy Council, and notification will be given to the League of Nations around March 10th to 15th. In addition, due to the importance of the issues of mandated territories, the Labor Conference, and the Economic Conference, related ministries have been ordered to investigate as soon as possible. Some cabinet members advocate that the Labor Conference and the Disarmament Conference should continue to be attended from a different standpoint. Roughly speaking, among the four disarmament representatives, Ambassador Matsudaira to the UK will remain until the end to observe the trend of the conference. The other three representatives, such as Ambassador Sato, and the military plenipotentiaries Tatekawa and Nagano, will each return to their posts and to their home countries. (26th Dentsu Dispatch)

Will Not Resign Due to Withdrawal from League of Nations

He also said that the election of judges to the Permanent Court does not involve the issue of nationality. The United States, although not a member of the League of Nations, has been elected three times. Brazil and Spain have both withdrawn from the League of Nations, but their judges did not resign, which can serve as precedents. (25th Reuters Dispatch)

A Certain Important Official Discusses the League of Nations' Handling of the Sino-Japanese Case

The Reason for the Sudden Change in Attitude of Britain and France

The Chinese People Should Have an Even Stronger Resolve in the Future

(Geneva) A certain important official of our delegation said that the report of the Nineteen-Member Committee was finally deemed fair and impartial by the General Assembly yesterday and was passed in its entirety. This was something that was unimaginable three months ago. Our side's hard work and patience were not in vain. It is regrettable that the League of Nations failed to take decisive action at the beginning of the Sino-Japanese dispute, leading to the deterioration of the situation and causing huge losses to China. When China submitted the case to the Executive Yuan, the attitude of various countries was mostly noncommittal. Even during the special session of the General Assembly in November, there were great differences in opinions between small and large countries. At that time, the pro-Japanese side, led by Simon, had a bad outlook. However, Japan's obstinacy and hypocrisy aroused dissatisfaction among the Nineteen-Member Committee, and their attitude suddenly turned tough. The League of Nations had no choice but to decide to condemn Japan. In addition to the aforementioned situation, factors that contributed to the passage of this report included the resumption of diplomatic relations between China and Russia, the United States' wholehearted cooperation with the League of Nations, and the dangerous development of the European political landscape. For example, the widely publicized secret pact between Germany and Italy made Britain and France feel greatly uneasy and deeply aware of the need to uphold the alliance and strengthen the League of Nations' reputation, which was also a major reason for promoting the League of Nations' determination. Now the whole world is on China's side rather than Japan's. We should also show the world a strongest determination to prove that China can not only resist aggressors but also has the power to drive them out of the country. If we do not work hard, there is little hope of recovering our homeland. The greater the sacrifice, the greater the gain. The opposite is also true. Heaven helps those who help themselves. Japan's abandonment by the whole world is the greatest opportunity for the Chinese people to strive for self-reliance. (Central News Agency dispatch, 25th)

Soviet Union Eliminates Homeless Children

(TASS) Moscow - The Soviet Union has recently eliminated homeless children without exception. Previously, there were 100,000 homeless children. They have now been placed in children's homes, and such wandering children are no longer seen on the streets and at doorways. These children were created by imperialist infighting and civil war, and they were homeless, living entirely by begging and stealing. The Soviet government considers these children to be a serious hindrance to society and is therefore striving to eliminate them. In 1919, the People's Committee resolved that the state would provide meals for all children under the age of 14 and built many children's homes to provide them with accommodation. In 1923, the "[Improving Children's Lives Lenin" Fund]] was established, the purpose of which was to reduce homeless children. To date, expenditure on this purpose has reached 137 million rubles, excluding donations from other organizations. Former homeless children have become educated citizens. All children are educated and given occupations. The Vormsok Children's Rehabilitation Center has 40 cattle, 18 horses, 30 sheep, 20 hectares of arable land, and more than a dozen stores. Most children's rehabilitation centers have achieved good results, with the largest producing several thousand rubles annually. The Kharkov Children's Rehabilitation Center can manufacture excellent cameras. The Bosheviki Rehabilitation Center near Moscow has the best results, producing millions of rubles annually. Foreign delegations regard this as a surprising success of the Soviet government. The Soviet Union's achievement in eliminating homeless children is worthy of being the world's first.

Deng Wen, Commander of the First Army of the Black Army, Telegraphs for Assistance

Horses Without Saddles, Men Barefoot and Unkempt

Urgently Awaiting Replacements to Fight the Enemy to the Death

Deng Wen, commander of the First Army of Ma Zhanshan's Black Army, telegraphed Ma General's representatives in Shanghai, Duan Zhongfan and Wu Huanzhang, after leading his troops from Heilongjiang to the border of Rehe, as the Japanese again launched a large-scale invasion of Rehe. His army bore the brunt, but the replacements had not yet been completed, and they were extremely distressed. He requested assistance. The original telegram is transcribed below: "Duan Zhongfan and Wu Huanzhang, brothers, to the Northeast Volunteer Army Relief Association, Chu Huiseng, and all directors, may it come to your attention: The Japanese bandits are wreaking havoc and forcibly occupying the Northeast. Chairman Ma Zhanshan led the brave soldiers of our Heilongjiang Province, upholding the banner of righteousness alone and fighting the Japanese enemy to the death, setting an example for the world. However, Heilongjiang Province, a poor and barren land, how can it withstand the wealth of the entire Japanese nation? Its inevitable defeat was expected by Wen and others. When the Soviet army was suddenly defeated and our contact was cut off, Wen followed Chairman Ma's order and transferred to Rehe, fighting thousands of miles for two months. More than a thousand officers and soldiers died under the enemy's gunfire, and six or seven hundred died of cold and starvation. This situation has been reported previously. Now that the brutal Japanese disregard international justice and are not subject to the restraints of justice, and are launching a large-scale attack on Rehe, North China is in turmoil, and the Black Army is once again bearing the brunt. Wen should continue to uphold Chairman Ma's original intention of fighting hard to reverse the decline, and it is his unshirkable responsibility to fight the Japanese to the death. However, our tens of thousands of brave soldiers who have fought for years, traveled thousands of miles, braved death, and sacrificed themselves for the country now have no pay and no clothes to cover their bodies. Moreover, the horses are without saddles and the men are barefoot and unkempt, like prisoners. As a commander, how can Wen drive them to fight? I cannot bear to drive them to their deaths. Those who came earlier have not fully changed their clothes, and those who come later may be even more disheartened. Therefore, I hereby telegraph to you to ask for further assistance, such as military uniforms, shirts, socks, boots, cotton blankets, saddles, large and small radio and telephone equipment, and heavy-duty vehicles, so that the morale of the soldiers can be boosted, our army's punitive power can be increased, the ugly captives can be wiped out, and our homeland can be restored. This will not only be deeply appreciated by all the officers and soldiers of our army, but also benefit the future of the country. The Commander of the First Army of Heilongjiang, Deng Wen, bows in respect."

River Shipping Companies Unite

Resisting the Monopoly of Foreign Merchant Ships

When the Sichuan war occurred last year, large quantities of textiles and cotton yarn ordered by Chongqing, Xupu, and other ports in Shanghai were stopped from being shipped and were stockpiled in Shanghai. Later, as the river water receded, the goods were still not shipped. Recently, as the Sichuan gangs' customers learned that the war had stopped and the upstream water was gradually increasing, they feared that traffic on the Yangtze River would be obstructed, so they telegraphed Shanghai to rush the shipment of goods. This caused a trend of foreign merchant ships competing to load and monopolize, and Chinese ships united to resist. The general situation is reported as follows:

Foreign Ships Compete for Shipping

Last year, due to the war in Sichuan, the goods accumulated in Shanghai were mostly foreign cloth and cotton yarn. Recently, Sichuan gangs have repeatedly telegraphed Shanghai to ship the goods to prevent traffic on the Yangtze River from being obstructed. The yarn and cloth are transported by two routes of merchant ships: one is a direct ship from Shanghai to Chongqing, and the other is a ship from Shanghai to Yichang, which is then transferred to Chongqing. The foreign merchants in Shanghai who specialize in Sichuan river shipping, the Jiejiang Company, have a total of twelve ships, followed by Taikoo Jardine, which also has more than ten ships. Now, the Jiejiang Company is competing to carry the cargo directly to Chongqing, and Taikoo Jardine is distributing the cargo to Yichang for transshipment. The competition has now started.

Increase in Water Rates

The main cargo for Sichuan river transportation is cotton yarn. Over the years, foreign ships have drastically reduced water rates in order to defeat Chinese merchant ships, reducing them to as low as six taels of silver per piece in the shortest time, causing many Sichuan river shipping companies, such as the Chuyun Company, to suspend operations. Based on the success of the price reduction strategy, foreign merchants gradually increased the freight rates again in the autumn and winter of last year. Cotton yarn water rates rose from six taels to eight taels, then from eight taels to ten taels, and then from ten taels to twelve taels, more than doubling. Special water rates are also required during shallow water.

Chinese Ships Unite

Last year, seven or eight small Sichuan river shipping companies were squeezed out by foreign ships and went bankrupt. At that time, the Chinese merchant Minsheng Company raised capital and bought all the suspended ships in order to consolidate the scattered forces and prevent the Sichuan river shipping rights from falling entirely into the hands of foreigners. The Minsheng Shipping Company then suddenly rose up and launched Shanghai-Chongqing, Shanghai-Yichang, Hankou-Yichang, and Xupu routes, with a total of more than ten ships, including the Minquan and Minzhu, to compete with Jiejiang and other foreign merchants. This time, when the Sichuan gangs rushed to load the accumulated goods, foreign ships took the opportunity to raise water rates. The Minsheng Company then united with the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, Sanbei, Yongxing, and Jiejiyuyu and other Chinese shipping companies to form the Sichuan River Chinese Ship Alliance, gathering strength to regain shipping rights, breaking the monopoly of foreign ships, and agreeing to reduce water rates for goods shipped from Shanghai to various parts of Sichuan from March 1st. The Shanghai branch notified the customer that yesterday, the foreign shipping companies in the city received an urgent telegram from Yichang, reporting that the Chinese ship union had been established and was completely to resist foreign merchant ships, and that they should quickly seek to salvage the situation. Each foreign merchant obtained the report and has been secretly discussing countermeasures.

Japanese Cause Trouble, Japanese Police Commit Violence

The Mainland News reports that at 5:50 p.m. yesterday, a Japanese man driving a cargo truck hit a Chinese pedestrian on Dalianwan Road and tried to escape. A Chinese policeman from a certain station saw this and quickly blew his whistle to stop him. Immediately, many Chinese people gathered. A young man described what he had seen of the accident. Suddenly, a Japanese policeman on the scene stepped forward and slapped him on the cheek. The crowd was outraged and surrounded the Japanese policeman and prevented the cargo truck from escaping. Other police officers rushed to the scene and dispersed the crowd. The injured Chinese man was taken to Sacred Heart Hospital by the fire brigade's ambulance. It is reported that he was injured in both legs and abdomen.

The Work and Organization of the Northeast Association

Soliciting Members in Two Weeks, Regular Meeting Tomorrow

The Northeast Association is a unified organization for rescuing the Northeast and studying the Northeast. Its purpose is to assist the soldiers fighting in the Northeast, investigate the current and past situation of the three eastern provinces, study the solution to the Northeast problem, and unite national organizations to jointly assist in exerting the perseverance and determination of the entire nation to solve the Northeast problem. At the beginning of its establishment, initiators Wu Tiecheng, Shi Liangcai, and others had clearly declared its purpose. Yesterday, all the directors of the association jointly declared, detailing the purpose of its establishment and the heavy responsibilities it bears, in order to awaken the people of the country to unite and carry out a total national mobilization to achieve its purpose. A Central News Agency reporter, in order to understand the current status of the association's planning and organization, visited the association's Secretary-General Zang Qifang, who gave him a detailed answer as follows:

Two Important Tasks

Zang told the reporter that the purpose of the establishment of the Northeast Association has been detailed in the declaration issued yesterday, and the people of the country should already understand it. What we are planning now is the work plan, the most important of which are two points: (1) How to enable the volunteer armies in the Northeast to fight together under unified leadership to respond to the national army; (2) To investigate the current situation of the three eastern provinces and the internal situation of the puppet organizations and Japan in order to study countermeasures. After Ma Zhanshan, Feng Zhanhai, Ding Chao, Li Du, and others successively left the country last year, the momentum of the Northeast Volunteer Army seemed to have subsided. However, in reality, no fewer than 200,000 people in the Northeast are waiting for orders, but they are hiding in the deep mountains to wait for an opportunity, either due to lack of leadership or because supplies have been cut off. Moreover, due to the strict investigation by the Japanese military police, domestic news cannot be conveyed there, so although they are ready, they do not yet know that the time to kill the enemy and serve the country has matured. Now that the great war on the border of Rehe has broken out, it is a good opportunity for the volunteer army to rise up in response and attack its rear. If the national army in Rehe Province can maintain it for three months, Japan's disastrous defeat will be within expectation. Even if Rehe Province unfortunately falls, the association's support for the volunteer army will not be reduced at all, because the effectiveness of the volunteer army fighting within its territory is greater than sending troops to recover the lost land. Therefore, on the one hand, the association must provide it with leadership and assistance, and on the other hand, it must transmit various messages to it, so that it can rise up in response at the right time.

Soliciting Members in Two Weeks

Continuing to talk about soliciting

members, Zang said that the

planning of the association's

affairs will be completed in

about two weeks, so the membership

In order to complete the Yuehan Railway, the Ministry of Railways requested the Sino-British Boxer Indemnity Committee to issue bonds worth 1.2 million pounds. After repeated discussions by the Sino-British Boxer Indemnity Committee and the approval of the guarantee issue, it is now known that it can be implemented soon. Government Determined to Reform the Currency System

Preparation for Bimetallism to Start on March 1st

The Money Trade Association Specially Held a General Meeting to Discuss It Yesterday

To Be Announced After Passed by the Central Political Council on the 28th

Since last year, the Ministry of Finance has organized a committee to specialize in research and planning for the implementation of currency reform and the abolition of silver and the adoption of the yuan. In early February, Finance Minister Song Ziwen and leaders of the silver and money industry agreed to start bimetallism on March 1st, and to completely abolish the silver system by July 1st. Leaders of the money industry, Yu Zuoting and Qin Qiqing, told a reporter from the New Sound Agency this morning that Finance Minister Song had talked to the leaders of the money industry about the Ministry of Finance's determination to reform the currency system, and the preparations and opinions of the money industry. At 3 p.m. yesterday, the money industry held a meeting of member representatives to discuss and decide on various matters, which are recorded separately below.

Government Resolution

Finance Minister Song Ziwen in Shanghai

On the 23rd, he met with leaders of the money industry, expressing the Ministry of Finance's determination to reorganize the currency system. Abolishing the tael and adopting the yuan must be implemented. The money industry also deeply understands the government's painstaking efforts and is determined to comply as scheduled. The period for both taels and yuan to be used concurrently is confirmed as March 1st, which must be submitted for approval at the Central Political Conference on the 28th of this month before being officially announced by the National Government.

Raw Silver Loan

The draft currency system regulations has also been

completed by the Ministry of Finance and will be submitted to the Central Political Conference on the 28th for approval and then submitted to the Legislative Yuan for discussion, approval, and promulgation. The Ministry of Finance is still in the process of securing a currency system loan of 500 million ounces of raw silver from the United States to reorganize the currency system and mint new coins.

Three Banks' Regulation

Starting next month, the concurrent use of taels and yuan

will be implemented, with the exchange rate set at 71.5. Subsequently, the exchange rate for foreign cents will no longer fluctuate daily. However, foreign banks still use silver taels as their standard, so foreign trade still requires the use of silver taels. The former exchange rate for foreign cents, which fluctuated based on supply and demand, will be abolished, and the Central Bank of China, the Bank of China, and the Bank of Communications will be responsible for regulation. Merchants who need silver taels can purchase them from the aforementioned three banks at the official exchange rate. However, if silver yuan are insufficient, silver taels can be minted. If silver taels are insufficient and silver yuan are used for reminting, there will be a loss of 1-2%. The Ministry of Finance has prepared to compensate for this loss.

Increased Foreign Exchange

Yesterday afternoon at 3:00 PM, the Money Industry

Association held a members' representative meeting and resolved that, starting from March 1st, in addition to the existing silver exchange, a foreign exchange would be added. The silver and foreign currencies will continue to exist concurrently on their respective standards. The implementation of a unified silver-yuan exchange rate will await the government's official announcement before it is dispersed. It is expected that starting from July 1st, the silver tael standard will be abolished, and all will be converted to silver yuan.

Two Industries' Opinions

Regarding the opinions of the silver and money industries on abolishing the tael and adopting the yuan,

the banking industry naturally expresses strong support. The money industry is quite concerned about whether silver yuan will be sufficient for application, and whether the minting capacity of the Central Mint can meet the needs of social finance. Actual experience will only be gained after a trial period. If there are no major obstacles, they will also agree.

Three New Managers Sheng Yun Appeal Acquittal

Managerial Remuneration Distribution Right to Discretion

Former manager of the Three New Cotton Mill, Sheng Yu Yun, sold scrap copper, etc. when the mill was sold, and instructed the general manager Sun He Cai to distribute 30,000 yuan to various employees as remuneration. Later, due to uneven distribution, a case arose in which the mill's employees Yu He Sheng, Yu Guo Xiang, and Chen Zhu sued Sheng for embezzlement in the First Special Court. The trial result considered Sheng to be suspected of breach of trust and sentenced him to a fine of 300 yuan. Sheng did not accept the judgment and appealed to the Second Branch of the High Court, which overturned the original judgment and declared him not guilty. This case is of great importance regarding the method of managers distributing employee remuneration in the business community. Here, we specially select and record the reasoning for the judgment of the First Branch of the High Court, copied below: The old iron and scrap copper owned by the Three New Textile Company in this case were sold entirely by the mill's general manager, Sun He Cai, and the sales price obtained, except for one account of Zhu Dao Ji, which had a small difference of one cent compared to the amount received in the bill, was consistent with the number of accounts received and distributed, as confirmed by the original auditor. In the report, regarding the expenditure section, although receipts were not obtained for payments to Chen Zhu Ting, Yu He Sheng, Yu Zi Sheng, Gu Yong Lan, Shao Chang Chun, Sun Yi, etc., Sun He Cai explained in the original trial the reasons why receipts could not be obtained. Chen Zhu Ting did not deny that he received 48 yuan of first-class money, and Yu Zi Sheng also stated that he received 200 yuan and 550 yuan, and that there were no receipts. Therefore, it is difficult to say that the various payments made by Sun without receipts were false. Even if there are inaccuracies, the sale of waste materials and the receipt and disbursement of money were handled by Sun alone and have nothing to do with Sheng Yu Yun. This point was also clearly admitted by Yu Guo Xiang. At most, it can only be said that Sheng Yu Yun did not fully exercise his supervisory duties. How can it be considered joint embezzlement or breach of trust? Moreover, since the appellants withdrew the part of the lawsuit against Sun He Cai and did not want to investigate further, they instead requested relief from the Social Affairs Bureau for Sheng Yu Yun, who was suspected of a lesser offense, and then filed a lawsuit with the original trial. After the judgment, they also appealed because the sentence was too light. What is their intention? It is even more difficult to understand. Furthermore, Sheng Yu Yun approved 2,000 yuan of foreign currency to Sun He Cai and distributed the remaining 861 yuan and 17 cents. Sun's remuneration was indeed much higher than that of other employees, but he held the position of general manager, and his seniority was also deeper than that of other employees. This time, he was able to recover the sales price of the waste materials that the mill had already sold, which helped the old employees, all because of Sun's negotiations with the buyer, as evidenced by Wu Kun Sheng's reply letter. Sheng Yu Yun, as the manager, did not want to share in the profits himself and gave 2,000 yuan to Sun He Cai, who had made special contributions, and distributed the remaining money to him as remuneration. It cannot be said that it was not fair and reasonable. According to a survey by the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce, the manager has the right to discretion in the distribution of employee remuneration, which is a common practice in commercial affairs, and there is no criminal suspicion whatsoever. The original judgment used this point as the basis for convicting Sheng Yu Yun of breach of trust, which is a mistake. Based on the above conclusions, the defendant's appeal in this case is justified, and although the appellants' appeal is not justified, part of the original judgment is also inappropriate. That part is revoked, and the defendant Sheng Yu Yun should be acquitted in accordance with Articles 379, 357, and 316 of the Criminal Procedure Law, and the judgment should be made in accordance with Article 385, Paragraph 1 of the same law. Presiding Judge Yu Hua, Judges Zhao Zheng Tang, Zhou Han.

Amateur Chat

The Final Resistance

— Duo Fei

Japanese imperialists are occupying our Manchuria with brutal force, bombing our Shanghai, coveting our Rehe, and recently advancing into Guannei, capturing our Shanhaiguan and Jiunmenkou, and threatening our Tianjin and Beijing; making all our people deeply feel that national demise is imminent, and everyone must unite and rise up to make a final and desperate resistance against our strong enemy.

What should we shop assistants do in this critical situation?

Some people say: "We shop assistants are suffering from economic oppression, and are struggling hard for our personal lives. No one cares about the rise and fall of the nation." You must know that when the country is truly lost and we become subjugated people, even if we can live in shame and humiliation, such a life is meaningless. It would be better to die happily!

Someone asks: "The Jewish people have no country, but they still live in the world, don't they?" You must know that the Jewish people are the most intelligent people in the world. Because they have no country and cannot get national protection, they are envied and persecuted everywhere in the world. Now they want to restore their country, but they cannot. Before the world reaches the Datong (Great Harmony), the country is the group where our nation entrusts its life, and we must never allow others to infringe upon it, and we must swear to protect it to the death. Because China lacks organization and does not know how to unite, the nation is still despised and abused everywhere. If even the country is lost, then the suffering of our Chinese nation in the future will be many times greater than that of the Jewish people! The Koreans and Indians of today are a great mirror for us Chinese.

Someone asks: "We shop assistants have no strength or courage. How can we love the country? How can we resist Japan?" You must know that resisting Japan does not mean that everyone in the country should carry a gun to the front line to fight. As long as everyone does their best within the scope of their ability, that's enough. "Boycotting Japanese goods" is a tactic that we shop assistants can do. If everyone does not buy or sell Japanese goods, it can greatly打击 Japanese imperialists' commerce and increase economic panic,促成 their imperialism's own collapse and demise.

Someone asks: "We can manage not to buy Japanese goods ourselves, but if our shop owners are greedy for profits and secretly import Japanese goods, and we shop assistants object and refuse to sell them, won't we be fired?" You must know that the phrase "do not buy Japanese goods" is not just a matter of saying it, but must be put into practice! If we buy one piece of Japanese goods, it is tantamount to giving the enemy some money to make more bullets and kill more of our soldiers on the front line. If the shop owner is greedy for profits and forgets morality and secretly imports Japanese goods, it will not succeed without our shop assistants helping him to do evil. If we and our fellow shop assistants do not help him do this treacherous deed, the shop owner can't do anything to us, and he will never dare to fire us for this reason. If we find out that he has this shameless behavior of secretly importing Japanese goods, we can send a secret letter to the organs responsible for sanctions, so that he has no way to use his tricks. This is the lowest minimum method for us shop assistants to love the country and resist Japan. If you still say that you can't do it, then I'm sorry! Prepare to be a subjugated people! Prepare to be a subjugated people of Japanese imperialists! Prepare your children and grandchildren to be subjugated people of Japanese imperialists forever!

Business and Industry Life

The Life of a Small Bank Clerk Snorting Among Banknotes

[When counting banknotes,] treat it as a snack. This is not a game. Each bill is five or ten yuan. If the amount is wrong, you have no say, you have to pay out of your own pocket. The first time you do this, you have to be extra careful." Old Wu told him.

"What are you afraid of? I don't intend to steal, how can the number be wrong?" He raised his head and answered, and followed Old Wu into the banknote room with a straight body. The banknote room was on the basement floor, surrounded by gray-white terrazzo. Except for three or four small iron windows, half exposed above the ground, the rest was dark and could not get a ray of light. The electric light shone brightly. On the damp floor, white wooden boxes squatted quietly one by one. Red and green banknotes were tightly bound with hemp rope, bundle after bundle like bundles of straw paper. Stacked on the table, you couldn't see the person opposite.

"So many!" He couldn't help but shout.

"This can be considered a lot. You haven't seen the banknote boxes in the vault, stacked on top of each other, like matchboxes in a杂货舖." Old Wu patted his shoulder with a smile and said.

"Damn it!" He said angrily in a low voice, as if expressing extreme injustice. "Poor people open their eyes wide like copper bells, and can't even get one bill all year round…"

"Say less!" Old Wu pulled his collar, and he didn't speak. They walked into another room, where several desks were placed horizontally and vertically. He sat down opposite Old Wu's desk. The things on the table were very simple: a pair of scissors, a glue jar, a few bundles of hemp rope, a green water pot with a sponge, and dozens of small white papers like tofu cubes. According to Old Wu, these were all the tools used when counting banknotes.

"Be careful when counting, this is 10,000 yuan in full." Old Wu handed over a banknote and instructed him, "After you count it, stack it in bundles of 5,000, tie it tightly with hemp rope, stick a square piece of paper on the knot, sign your name, and you will be responsible for the amount of this bundle of banknotes."

"I know." He answered, then cut the hemp rope with scissors, took out a stack, held the corners of the banknotes with both hands, and counted them rustlingly. He was very careful, because the hard banknotes were slippery to count. After counting one hundred, he wondered if there was one missing, so he took it over and counted it again.

"Slowly, the banknotes are slippery, you can dip some water before counting." Old Wu raised his head and said, "Counting banknotes is not easy! We are fine, we are already skilled at counting, we can count even with our eyes closed. Not to mention, how many tens of millions of banknotes have we counted?" As he said, a smug smile appeared on his face.

"Tens of millions?"

"This is not bragging to you, tens of millions are enough, but it's always someone else's. After counting until now, I only made my fingers thick and big. I often think, if I have nothing to do in the future, I'll go back and count straw paper." Old Wu was a little emotional.

He had counted four thousand, and there were still several stacks of uncounted on the table. He didn't know how many more there were. He only felt that there were more and more of them. At the same time, the air was suffocating, and his breathing was a little rapid. He couldn't take a breath of fresh air. However, the nauseating musty smell, mixed with the fermented smell of glue, was still constantly being sent into his nostrils. It was as if a lead cake was pressing on his heart, gradually becoming heavier! His brain was also swelling. He regretted coming here. He thought that a man should stand in a bright and upright place and do something refreshing. But now he was hiding in this dark banknote room, unable to breathe even a little free air, it was too suffocating! "Damn it," who is patient enough to do this unpromising thing! He cursed secretly. He really wanted to drop the banknotes and quit, but that would break his rice bowl. Old Wu, who was sitting in front of him, seemed to know his thoughts, so he sighed and said to him: "Eating this bowl of rice is not just suffering, but also being worried all day long. A little carelessness will cost you money. Sometimes, even if you count carefully yourself, others will accuse you, saying that so and so much is missing from the banknotes you handled. Losing money is nothing, but you will also get a bad name. But we know the suffering here, and we are still willing to do this. It seems that we don't care about missing banknotes, losing money, or bad reputation. You will be the same as me if you work here for a long time. Aren't there many students who graduated from your school who come here? Some people would rather not study, and want to cross this threshold, but can't cross it. Everyone wants to come to the bank to make a fortune... make a fortune... make a fortune... Of course, there are also those who make a fortune, but only…"

He felt that Old Wu's words were very good, and he himself had come with this kind of thinking. He heard those

Page 22

People who have earned some money in the bank say that the bank is such a good place, there are almost 洋錢鈔票 everywhere, you eat well, and there are also bonuses at the end of the year. As long as you are honest and hardworking, you can definitely be promoted to teller, director, and manager step by step, and you will have a very good future. This kind of rumor grabbed the heart of his aging mother, so she persuaded him, and made him also dream of making a fortune. But what exactly is the benefit that others talk about? The job he was doing was only a four-yuan-a-month trainee, squatting in this stuffy room counting banknotes all day long. Others had never told him this before, and he was now starting to doubt it.

"What's wrong? You can't count anymore!" Old Wu asked him in surprise: "Dinner is coming soon, count quickly, don't waste any more time."

Hearing Old Wu's words, he was startled, as if he had just woken up from a dream. He didn't answer, and didn't think anymore, and continued to count.

After dinner, they continued to count banknotes, and their hands and feet were very fast. He understood that this was the result of his first job, and it was also the beginning of his future. He thought, if his two hands turned into a living machine, then banknotes would fly out of his hands like a general, and hundreds of thousands, or even a box, could be counted quickly in a day. In this way, his dream would come true. Raise salary, promote to director, promote to manager, golden rays of light floated before his eyes. Count! Count! An unstoppable desire shouted in his chest. He felt that his whole body was activated. He rolled up his sleeves, took a stack of banknotes in his hands, and counted them one by one. He was sweating from counting, but he still kept counting.

"Count slowly, it's easy to be wrong if you go too fast." Old Wu called to him from across the room. So he stopped and turned to look at Old Wu. Old Wu still had his head down. The thin face where you could see the cheekbones, was covered with blue veins, all trembling slightly.

"You have this little bit left? You count so fast!" Old Wu asked him with a smile. He nodded with a smile.

"If you work so hard, you may be promoted quickly in the future. But that's how it is here, the ones with big backgrounds, the ones who flatter well, get a salary increase of dozens of dollars at once. The ones who bury their heads in their work without saying a word get at most four洋. I have been working here for almost ten years, and I only have twenty-odd yuan in salary. May I ask, how can I maintain such a high cost of living, with a large family and often being sick? I have no other choice, otherwise, I would not be willing to be here." Old Wu's words were simply a basin of cold water, extinguishing the flames of his desire.

"Really?" He asked in fear.

"What am I lying to you for? I'll tell you, there's another thing that's sad to talk about. There used to be an Old Zhang here, who was already in his twenties. When he came, he was also a four-dollar trainee, counting banknotes here. He was very honest. One time, he was careless, and the banknotes he was given didn't add up to the right number. When he counted them at night, he was short a thousand. The manager told him to pay it back, and if he didn't pay it back, he would be fired and he would have to take out the money to pay it back. He desperately scraped together a few hundred yuan at home, so he wasn't fired. He often told people that he had been wronged to death, and he couldn't say anything about it. He was willing to pay off the money and quit, even if he had to beg for a living. He later worked really hard, using his dinner money, not eating, gnawing on sesame cakes, and washing his own clothes. When he came, he had a smiling, white and fat face, but later he became much thinner and yellow, and he got the disease of spitting blood. Last year, he finally paid off the money and returned to his hometown. I don't know what happened to him later, but someone said that he was dead…"

At this time, his mood had changed. The previous hope had disappeared. On the one hand, physical fatigue, and on the other hand, Old Wu's words deprived him of his fantasies. Regardless of whether Old Wu was joking with him, Old Wu himself was an example. Did he make a fortune? Did he get promoted to manager? Not at all. After ten years of hard work, the result was a body with the symptoms of tuberculosis. Would he get the same result as Old Wu in the future? Who can say no? Thinking of this, he felt more and more uneasy in his heart. Sadness and terror occupied his mind, and his mind was confused, reflecting scene after scene: "Banknote room... missing banknotes... losing money... bad reputation... dismissal... getting tuberculosis... grave..." He felt that the future was full of danger, and he was terrified. He had no energy to count the remaining hundreds of banknotes on the table. It was still Old Wu calling to him from across the room: "Don't be in a daze, it's getting late, let's get back to work!" His mind became clear, and he lowered his head.

Amateur Study Shop Assistants

What Novels Should You Read?

— Father

Put aside "Jianghu Knight Errant" and "The Smiling, Proud Wanderer,"

Read books like "The Trilogy" and "The Iron Flood"!

Shop assistants often pick up a novel to pass the time when they are free. Among these recreational readings, according to my recent findings, "Jianghu Knight Errant" and "The Smiling, Proud Wanderer" are the most popular.

The reason why shop assistants like to read "Jianghu Knight Errant" and "The Smiling, Proud Wanderer" is the same reason why petty citizens like to watch horror movies with animal scenes, that is, "escaping reality."

Shop assistants belong to the petty bourgeoisie of society. The petty bourgeoisie is fundamentally a shaky and uneasy class. Of course, there are very few who can be lucky enough to climb to a high level and become a true bourgeoisie, but most are still shaky, uneasy, bitter, and without a way out, and finally disillusioned and declined!

We who are shaky, uneasy, bitter, and without a way out, especially those of us who are born in modern China, because of various other reasons, are even more dissatisfied with reality, and the mood of bitterness and helplessness is particularly high. As a result, we go to books that are 180,000 miles away from actual life and years away from the times to find another world, a moment of illusion and an inexplicable rose-colored dream. Therefore, "Jianghu Knight Errant" and "The Smiling, Proud Wanderer" are very popular.

But what exactly do these books give us? That is nothing more than the sadness after the illusion and the nightmare after the dream.

With piles

Could Automatic Machines Replace Shop Assistants?

— Zu Tong

Recently, automatic machines have been innovated in many ways. Some dispense a piece of candy for a penny, while others dispense a one-cent postage stamp for a one-cent coin. Scholars who are fascinated by machines have proposed installing automatic machines in various shops to replace shop assistants. This kind of prejudice is understandable if shop assistants can only handle straightforward transactions. In that case, it is more economical to use machines than to hire shop assistants. However, not all transactions are as simple as selling candy and postage stamps, so shop assistants cannot be entirely abolished and still have a value that should be maintained. I will now elaborate on the reasons below:

(1) Guiding Customers: Customers may not fully understand the application of various goods in a shop. It is difficult to understand the underlying meaning without the repeated explanation of shop assistants. There is a Western saying: [Shopkeepers are the guides of the people, and the standard of living is promoted through them.] This is indeed a meaningful statement!

(2) Rooted in Habit: Customers enter the shop and see shop assistants, talk about transactions, and interact with each other. This has been a long-standing habit. Therefore, replacing shop assistants with machines is practically impossible.

(3) Selling Goods: Many goods cannot be sold by themselves. For example, insurance, sewing machines, and musical instruments, etc., cannot be sold without the promotion of shop assistants. When competition arises, it depends even more on the selling ability of shop assistants. Some people regard salesmen as commercial envoys, so the importance of shop assistants can be imagined!

(4) Increasing Prices: The value of goods often needs to be increased through good salesmanship. Shop assistants put in a lot of effort, and customers also find many uses for the goods, so they do not consider the increased price to be excessive.

(5) Attracting Customers: Good shop assistants have the ability to retain old customers and attract new ones. The shop's business depends entirely on maintaining this, making them indispensable talents for the time being. All that is left is despair, and the most is [boredom].

Therefore, we must immediately discard them and find readings that can shout out our bitterness, express our suffering, and provide us with solutions. Here, I will temporarily take Mao Dun's "Trilogy" and the foreign product "The Iron Flood" as representatives.

Mao Dun's "Trilogy" fully expresses the anxiety and decline of the petty bourgeoisie, and can indeed represent our voice, but unfortunately it is only [just that] and still has no way out and no solutions.

"The Iron Flood" is a foreign novel, and there is also a Chinese translation. This book is full of [power], [motion], and [struggle]. Its revelation is: [Struggle can survive,] An complacency is destruction. A group of people seeking survival are moving forward like iron, which is exactly a broad road for our survival.

Let's change the taste, I pray like this.

Sketches of a Waitress's Life by Shi Min

Self-Introduction for Job Seeking

May Tianfeng Jun Have a Smooth Journey

Self-Introduction for Job Seeking, Reply No. 4: Mr. Tianfeng, please indicate the required salary, working hours, age, and place of origin!

Wu Chan, Guanghua Machinery Dyeing and Weaving Factory, Nanluban Road, Lujiiawan, this city.

Speaking Out Against Injustice

— HCY

The Ratio of Two and Twenty: Is Justice Just?

I am a person who already has a job! Secretary of the XX Small Newspaper. Originally, in this year of oversupply of manpower, it is already very lucky to have a job; if you want to find another position, it seems inevitable to hope too much! But please forgive me, because the treatment I am receiving now is really too unfair.

I am from Haining, and I didn't know the XX Small Newspaper, but because I repeatedly contributed to the newspaper between last summer and autumn, I later wrote to the museum in a self-recommendation way to seek a position. Mr. Gongzheng, the manager, did not abandon me and ordered me to come to Shanghai, so I came to Shanghai to serve as a secretary. But the monthly salary is only one yuan, I still tolerate it first, thinking that the future may be hopeful; unexpectedly, it was not until this year that it increased by one yuan, and Secretary X, who does less than half of my work, has a monthly salary of twenty yuan, which inevitably makes me very disappointed and I have to make other plans.

I am seventeen years old this year and have a middle school education. My Chinese is still fluent and I can write essays of six or seven hundred words; I can read ordinary books and newspapers in English, and I am currently studying [Rhetoric and Composition] and [Advanced Translation] in the English Department of the Commercial Press Correspondence School. I am physically strong, do not smoke or drink; I can endure hardship and work hard.

The desired job is: a trainee in a company or a clerk in a commercial organization, or temporarily a trainee nature that can be promoted soon. As for the treatment, the minimum requirement must be able to provide food and accommodation and five or six yuan of pocket money per month (this refers to the temporary training period). Please forward correspondence to this publication.

Please Note, Unemployed Friends

Mr. Zheng Xingjian wrote a letter saying that he will make a considerable contribution to [general unemployment]. If you want to know the details, please attach two cents of postage and send a letter to No. 103, Lane 546, Tiantong Road to inquire.

Mr. He Xiyu has four children, all of whom are at the elementary level. He now wants to hire a tutor who must be proficient in Cantonese and teach two hours every night (7:00 to 9:00 pm). Mailing address: No. 113, Xinqingli, Lane 318, Tiantong Road, Hongkou.

Liangchen Hao You She, located at the intersection of Beijing Road and Zhejiang Road in this city, now wants to add five printing workers, paying based on the number of products produced. Any unemployed printing workers who are accustomed to using foot-operated small printing presses, are physically strong and hardworking, and have a certificate of good conduct from the previous employer, or can provide a guarantor from this city, can personally visit the society between 2 pm and 6 pm every day to discuss a trial job.

Shop Assistant Communication

A Small Boat Heavily Loaded

— Zhu Zengwei

Editor: Since your column was born, I have often seen apprentices in many shops saying that the boss or manager only knows how to call them as errand boys, and they have no opportunity to learn any practical business experience; this will of course disappoint them. But my situation is very different. I am only seventeen years old this year. Last September, I was introduced by relatives and friends to work in a yarn shop in this city. Half because I am a person who has already graduated from junior high school, and I can cope with ordinary writing and calculations, and I am not very stupid by nature, and I can learn everything; but half is also because my guarantor is very reliable; therefore, I am grateful to the boss for his excessive reuse. Less than a month after entering the shop, he taught me how to help with the accounts; later, the actual accounting officer, because his wife died, asked for leave to return to his hometown, and he honestly and rudely called me to act as his agent. Until the time of the big settlement, this actual accounting officer came to cancel his leave; in total, I acted as the accounting officer for about three months. During this period, partly because the boss was always by my side, and my colleagues did not dare to make things difficult for me; and partly because everything had the original accounting officer, who set up a scale, and I followed Xiao Gui Cao Sui, so there was no difficulty; so there were no mistakes. Now the boss has established a branch in another city, and the staff inside include newly arrived ones and those sent from the old shop; I, in fact, have been sent to be the accountant of the branch. The scale of the branch is certainly different from the main store, how can I handle it? My colleagues see that I am young and ignorant, and the boss is not by my side, so it is difficult to guarantee that they will not deliberately make things difficult. The accountant of the branch has a very high status and has full power; but the responsibility is also very serious, and I am the only one who will be asked. So I politely declined to the boss, so that I could learn for a few more years in front of the boss. Who knows, the old man did not think so, saying that I was unwilling to serve him because of the meager salary (five yuan per month), and I held a grudge. Ah! This is really unheard of! I am a student, and I am flattered to have five yuan income every month, how dare I complain? But a small boat is heavily loaded, and I really can't believe in myself! Is it better not to go, or is it better to go? Please, enlightened editor, make a decision for me. (To be continued) Zhu Zengwei respectfully submitted

Editor's note: It is certainly regrettable to use great talent for small things; but a small boat heavily loaded will inevitably capsize, which is very dangerous. Although Mr. Zhu said that he has a foundation in safe writing and calculation, his experience in the business world is too poor. In the main store, because there was a boss to guide him, he was fortunate not to fall, but now he is called to stand alone, how can that be possible? Fortunately, Mr. Zhu is self-aware and is not moved by vanity, which is indeed where he is superior. I hope he can be cautious to the end, and the boss will not stop his business because of this. At the same time, I hope his boss will allow Mr. Zhu's request and select capable personnel to handle the affairs of this branch. Then, not only can Mr. Zhu progress step by step and not have the danger of climbing high and falling hard, but the future of the branch is also more promising. If you insist on forcing Mr. Zhu to go and work hard, then Mr. Zhu will inevitably be sacrificed; although the guarantor is indeed reliable, I am afraid that he can be fully responsible for the boss's improper deployment.

Editor's Notes

The Dancing of Hands

The era is roaring, the whole world

is in a storm.

Every day, every day, I see many hands trembling and stretching out in front of me.

Those are not hands that stretch out for money and seek leisure without labor; nor are they hands that hold champagne glasses and play golf; nor are they lewd hands that live in grand hotels and make [night pilgrimages] on women's legs; alas! pitiful! Those are dry, trembling, gray-white, malnourished, cowardly hands! [Editor, please publish my manuscript in the self-introduction for job seeking column! I have been unemployed for a long time!] These hand brothers and sisters often say to me, with a pleading tone.

But please forgive me, forgive me, all you hardworking hands! Although I have disclosed your manuscripts, what can I do to help you? What does this dying society give you, except to put hunger, pain, oppression, and death in your hands? Among these hundreds of hands, I am afraid that less than one percent can find a job by luck through the power of newspapers! The rest are still idle, so empty as if they have lost something precious? Fortunately, what I can see and touch is only these hundreds of hands: if I add the hands of 30 million unemployed workers and hundreds of millions of other unemployed people in the world, I am afraid my eyes will be blinded! Every day, every day, I see many hands trembling and waving in front of me.

Pitiful! They are just getting smaller and smaller day by day, and are almost climbing to the hunger line! Sometimes, I really want to hold them and shed a tear of sympathy, but sometimes, I get angry.

[You stupid hands, haven't you turned over the map, don't you know that there is a country on this earth without unemployment, and there is still a shortage of millions of workers?] I think, but the great laws and religions are pressing on my head, I am afraid! I am afraid! Finally, I did not say it. I can only learn from the tone of imperialism and shout loudly: [The Soviet Union is a country of forced labor], don't believe it!]

Good [superiors] of the world! Please release some compassion and save these hands and ladies, help [hands]! Help [hands]! Look, they are not resisting you; they are the most docile, as if they have never clenched their fists, never returned hand for hand, and never [overthrown] anyone; they have long put aside all the oppression and pain they have suffered, and completely forgotten it! All cannons, airplanes, machine guns, and shrapnel are simply useless to them. They are just begging! Begging! Now, they are all quietly lying still on my desk, they will not [rebel], let alone [riot]. Look, how gentle they are, how lovely they are! But they are so small, so pitiful! Quick! Quick! Help [hands]! Help [hands]! Give them rice bowls! Oh, oh, look, look, one is already dead!

[Editor, my friend Mr. Zhihui sent a manuscript, which was published in the self-introduction for job seeking column, I am very grateful! But I have not received a reply for a long time, and I am very anxious. Now he suddenly committed suicide by jumping into the river the night before...]

Strangely enough, this world seems to only need those fat hands plated with gold.

Turn your hands! Turn your hands! Put your hands back! Put your hands back! Connect hands tightly with each other! All hardworking friends, please! please! please!

The era is roaring, the whole world is in a storm. (Editor)
